Good morning, [@Ssmiles](https://xdaforums.com/m/7087006/)

I've edited your above post and removed the reference to Telegram. Regarding social media please observe that as an exemption from the last bullet of rule no. 5 of the [XDA Forum Rules](https://xdaforums.com/t/xda-developers-forum-rules.4200559/), we grant only developers the privilege to share references to their social media in their **own development threads and if thorough support is provided in the thread.** These conditions obviously don't apply to this thread or generally to you and your posts. Additional information is also available here:

![xdaforums.com](https://xdaforums.com/data/assets/logo/header-forum.jpeg)

### Telegram Chat Channels - Way Forward

WhatsApp/Telegram Groups and Channels - Going Forward  Hello XDA family! Just notifying all members that posting certain links to Telegram and other sites like WhatsApp is now allowed on XDA.  What does that mean?  We will allow links to messages...

![xdaforums.com](https://xdaforums.com/data/assets/logo/favicon-32x32.png)

Please refrain from sharing references to social media in future unless done in your own development threads! Thanks for your cooperation.

Hey I know the OnePlus Nord n30 (when my RM7 died I had to let's not talk about it) the phone was like a maze to unlock boot loader. First you couldn't be in fastboot, had to be fastboot.d and the regular fastboot command wouldn't work it was instead another command. Any fastboot command If I remember correctly on that phone was dependant on what fastboot you were in. Fastboot was user space had limited access to flash a few things no more than updates tho and fastboot.d was the one with the ability.

Has anyone tried any thing yet I'll go ahead and be the tester. Even If I unlock the bl and get magisk installed I'd still want a custom recovery and those are the tricky thing

Also fwiw that check box for bootloader won't do anything you will notice but it allows the commands to unlock bootloader actual run. Perhaps different version or region

### #129 — **SYXZ** · Jul 21, 2025 at 8:36 PM · page 7

**Why most EDL tools get stuck or fail when flashing Redmagic 10** : The steps for edl writing are sending loader file, configuring port, and sending write commands. Red Magic 10 has modified the configure command, an additional **Oem="ZTE"** parameter must to be added to the normal command, otherwise an error will be returned: **Tool doesn't come from ZTE.** This issue needs to be resolved by the edl tool developer.

---

### #186 — **ks75vl** · Oct 23, 2025 at 9:40 AM · page 10

```
Python:

import base64
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import rsa
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import padding
from cryptography.hazmat.backends import default_backend
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes
import struct

eng_abl_extracted_pubkey = bytes.fromhex(
    "0000080032DED7A1C3F63D29B3321CB2AEC98A3E06355DECC852DD65547FCCBB85DB860EA5E8311AA57065EC186F32B18975B3E85A57AA1B9A0E13FB241439AD647D9D3B5F149AEB10D6C8CB1BE883FBB3644F5CE8C08E84A1C6349D9F3F830A3CCF5026FEE5E1D34531A1E9FAD33EF8219CFCA4C9CAF22656A422E36096A0DB1DF63BC927894C13E68022893365AB8EAC8421215EB3E4D8AEA5ADEBF9099EA8F92B044EAE16A5933622ADEAAB90FAD6FBF0C6D42C2370831E67020FC4A6314586D90281ECBE70529AB00748B7FD0FB093EB951EC4320B3BCB1D6B76FAF32F1EA1E117953B82D53038CF1CDC706A88540F7FDC6B363B7494C6600DC2D2780CBA5C583761E3C3339F29A7B62C5D3ED123B959E3C5DD2E8E4B841BA626AC71422FA0766252D8051FF491A789C4AE7505FB83E67C0429BF5AC85B6EE114CFED41BA45188966B9E3E1830858CAA34C995AF5FFC77B1C8B23066DC9A25C2E65DAA1A6A9360BB5A0B9DFF16B0A918EEDA35EA21D2097D982B8C5843F469A62C535C08310AD3D01022A431B7BF6B912DD00B4CD733C4E41DB1BDFB69E8B3FFE732A80BB6AB98289DB91F80F8DEACD9DE4F9DBF85C2EDE7EB02C4B4E120325A757B49A41BE18BF7A03C740D0C73F8E718B092CF67535FAB7E66D75FAAEC9A172A58D7CF14BEE114FE0C7133A4204B292B4FF404A8F03700EEB26E326FF997351F1E65B8901E4496E91DD0C45"
)

def ztecfg_get_string(key) -> bytes:
    # Get from zte.cfg, key-value store
    raise NotImplementedError

def ztecfg_get_int(key) -> int:
     # Get from zte.cfg, key-value store
    raise NotImplementedError

def BoardSerialNum() -> str:
    # From UEFI API: "EFI_STATUS BoardSerialNum (CHAR8 *StrSerialNum, UINT32 Len)""
    raise NotImplementedError

def custom_key_parser(a1_blob: bytes):
    """
    AI generated from decompiled code ( need confirmation )
    """
    if len(a1_blob) != 520:
        raise ValueError("A1 blob must be 520 bytes for a 2048-bit key.")

    # 1. Extract Exponent (E)
    exponent_bytes = a1_blob[4:8]
    e_int = struct.unpack('<I', exponent_bytes)[0]

    # 2. Extract Modulus (N)
    raw_modulus_data = a1_blob[8:264]

    # Check key size (optional, for verification)
    key_bits_le = a1_blob[0:4]
    key_bits = struct.unpack('<I', key_bits_le)[0] # 2048
    if key_bits != 2048:
        print(f"Warning: Key bits {key_bits} detected, expecting 2048.")

    WORDS_COUNT = 64
    WORD_SIZE = 4 # bytes

    # a) Split into 64 words
    words = [raw_modulus_data[i:i + WORD_SIZE] for i in range(0, 256, WORD_SIZE)]

    # b) Reverse the word order (reverses the custom word-reversal)
    words.reverse()

    # c) Byte-swap each word (reverses the bswap32) and concatenate
    final_modulus_bytes = b''
    for word in words:
        # '<I' reads the 4 bytes as a Little-Endian unsigned integer
        le_word_int = struct.unpack('<I', word)[0]

        # '>I' writes the integer as a Big-Endian word (bswap32 equivalent if starting from LE)
        be_word_bytes = struct.pack('>I', le_word_int)
        final_modulus_bytes += be_word_bytes

    # d) Convert the final Big-Endian byte array to an integer
    n_int = int.from_bytes(final_modulus_bytes, byteorder='big')

    return n_int, e_int

# Signature
signature = b""
for i in range(12):
    signature += ztecfg_get_string('deviceid.sign.{}'.format(i))

decoded_signature = base64.b64decode(signature)
print('decoded_signature =', decoded_signature.hex())

# Auth Type
auth_type = ztecfg_get_int('auth_type')

# Board Serial Number
board_sn = BoardSerialNum()

# Create data
data_to_hash = str(auth_type).zfill(8) + board_sn

# Check signature
N, E = custom_key_parser(eng_abl_extracted_pubkey)
public_numbers = rsa.RSAPublicNumbers(e=E, n=N)
public_key = public_numbers.public_key(backend=default_backend())

public_key.verify(
    signature=decoded_signature,
    data=data_to_hash,
    padding=padding.PKCS1v15(),
    algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
)

print("Signature is valid.")
```

I reviewed the abl_eng code, and the Fastboot unlock verification in the Python pseudocode seems to make sense, need more reverse to confirm

---

### #187 — **ks75vl** · Oct 23, 2025 at 7:57 PM · page 10

The pubkey in the abl_eng is protected by the primary bootloader. The associated data and signature are stored in ztecfg. It seem no legitimate tool exists to unlock the bootloader without access to the prikey and ztecfg permissions. Therefore, I suspect that any “unlock tool” likely exploits a vulnerability in the abl_eng to bypass these restrictions.

---

### #188 — **ks75vl** · Oct 24, 2025 at 2:46 PM · page 10

I have confirmed that the unlock verification uses RSA signature verification. The public key in the abl_eng follows the structure shown in the picture
![pubkey_structure.png](https://xdaforums.com/attachments/pubkey_structure-png.6282319/)

Also, I have successfully run the function using Unicorn.

![unicorn_output.png](https://xdaforums.com/attachments/unicorn_output-png.6282320/)

### #189 — **hoahenry** · Oct 24, 2025 at 3:23 PM · page 10

> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

I know some information, hope it will be useful for you:

- abl_eng is only a part, we also need to edit the ztecfg.img file

- When comparing between a ztecfg file of a device without bootloader unlocked and a file of a device with bootloader unlocked (unlocked by a service) by hex code, I see that it is edited from line 2000 onwards with encrypted data that is supposed to be built by uuid, serial or imei of the device (because each ztecfg.img file is edited for each device - cannot be shared).

- In this thread there is also a person who successfully flashed abl_eng and used ```fastboot flashing unlock``` but it failed (the script works but needs a few more things), this indicates that we just need to analyze abl_eng to see what it needs and then edit ztecfg.img and test again

### #196 — **ks75vl** · Oct 25, 2025 at 4:42 AM · page 10

> **hoahenry said:**
> What is this for?
>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

That is the signature verification. In RSA digital signature, the signer use private key to encrypt the hashed message, the verifier using public key to decrypt and get the hash, if that hash match with the message in verifier’s side, then signature is valid.

### #204 — **ks75vl** · Oct 26, 2025 at 4:32 AM · page 11

> **hoahenry said:**
> Hey I'm here with the original ztecfg of the device not yet unlocked bootloader.
>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

I’ve checked, and there’s no default value for the signature field. It seems the unlock serviceman has a method—possibly access to a private key or the signing API—to generate the signature for a new device.

Here’s a summary of what we know:

•  The ztecfg image contains an RSA signature for the device’s UFS serial number (starting with CRC32 + some known value).

•  The abl_eng bootloader verifies this signature before executing the unlock bootloader command.

I’ve noticed a file named devprog.melf, which I believe is related to Firehose, as it contains code from the Firehose library. Does anyone know how this file is used?

---

---

### #216 — **DarkestSpawn** · Oct 30, 2025 at 5:52 PM · page 11

> **AeroGami said:**
> How do you guys know the bootloader is unlocked? I bought and check it has bootloader unknown here.
>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

Settings->Developer Options:  look at OEM unlocking. If it's toggled on and greyed out, that's the easiest way to tell while booted. When rebooting, if you are greeted with your bootloader is unlocked warning that's the other easy way to tell.

Or if you know how to reboot to bootloader,  run this code from a cmd line with Googles adb tools:

```
Code:

fastboot getvar unlocked
```

or

```
Code:

fastboot getvar all
```

and look for "unlocked: "(there will be a yes or no after the colon)

---

### #232 — **BeFresh_** · Dec 4, 2025 at 6:15 PM · page 12

> **hoahenry said:**

>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

Booted in edl mode using adb, launched one of his tools (QLM), logged in using credentials then the app launched. His app had a menu where he could search for a specific phone model. Mine is Redmagic 10 Air (so NX779J) but he used Redmagic 10 Pro instead (NX789J). Once he selected the phone model, he read the partition table (he pressed a button named Read GPT) and then he had a button on his app "Unlock Bootloader" which sent a firehose. The other steps i don't know because it was done by his app (QLM), maybe you can find something in the app's logs (in the archive i sent you above, containing his tools).

### #233 — **BeFresh_** · Dec 4, 2025 at 6:16 PM · page 12

### #254 — **BeFresh_** · Dec 18, 2025 at 1:39 PM · page 13

You guys need a special QCOM driver for EDL mode, it should be somewhere in the files i sent but if not i'll try to find it and send it to you. What he just done for my Redmagic 10 Air was install that specific drivers version, boot in EDL, pressed Read GPT and then Unlock Bootloader. Then, my phone got out of EDL and screen was all black but in the Device Manager the phone wasn't in EDL mode anymore and it was recognized as Unknown Device. He right clicked on it, install drivers and chose ADB Drivers (If i remember correctly it was Android Boot Interface). Then my phone's screen turned on and asked if i was sure about unlocking bootloader with Yes and No options.

### #255 — **Reminon** · Dec 19, 2025 at 10:23 AM · page 13

>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

The Air can be unlocked like the 9s according to R2B. That's why yours was different.

I got mine unlocked tonight and he read my ztecfg partition, but stopped it before it finished dumping the whole partition. He got 432KB of the 512KB partition and apparently it was sufficient.

I'm sure somewhere in the chain he flashed a possibly rebuilt ztecfg partition, but it did not show it on my screen.

He just read mine, transferred the incomplete file to himself over ultra viewer, after about 10 minutes, he came back and clicked unlock bootloader.

My phone rebooted into fastboot where he did fastboot flashing unlock and the unlock menu appeared.

[@extra98](https://xdaforums.com/m/13313391/) you may have gotten QLM to work, but it cannot unlock the 10 pro or 10s bootloader by itself. It should be able to send a loader, backup and restore partitions, and maybe some other stuff.

[@mark332](https://xdaforums.com/m/8381290/) it does support the 10 pro and pro, but not by itself.

### #257 — **Reminon** · Dec 25, 2025 at 10:49 PM · page 13

I've been able to get twrp and ofrp to build and boot on the recovery partitions, but I haven't been able to get touch working yet. HW controls do work in ofrp, albeit it's rather finicky.

I've noticed that if the stock recovery is present, then the fastboot in bootloader mode doesn't allow me to switch slots or flash partitions that I've tried. It forces me to use fastbootd in the stock recovery. If I have a custom recovery installed, then the fastboot in bootloader mode seems to have full functionality.

"It's been a while since I've messed with a modern device, so this may be normal".

### #259 — **hoahenry** · Dec 30, 2025 at 7:59 AM · page 13

All devices require the `device.sign.*` string in the `ztecfg.img` file; it needs to be signed in some way that we don't yet know. Some models, like the 9s/Pro and 10 Air, already have these signatures in their `ztecfg.img` files (this is why they only need software and a bootloader unlock button – you can preview the file before unlocking to see).

My baby was born not long ago, so I need to dedicate my time to caring for him. I will learn more if I can. The rest will have to be left to others.

>
> Click to collapse

AVB is active and the system partition is R/O so root in that way isn't possible to my knowledge. With the bootloader locked, you can't tamper with the partitions that aren't AVB protected  " recovery, init_boot, etc.

If you are using [bkerler](https://github.com/bkerler/edl) EDL tool on linux, you need to add:

```
Code:

f"Oem=\"ZTE\" " + \
```
in "/edlclient/Library/firehose.py" at line 872 or 873 (I forget the exact line) where you installed bklerer EDL tool. I also had to add it to the "/usr/local/lib/python3.12/dist-packages/edlclient/Library/firehose.py" at the same line to get the EDL tool on Linux for it to work for some reason. This way I could use EDL.

No progress or Full Dump. Just pulled ztecfg to help work with getting it signed for bootloader unlocking.

On a different note, previously I was trying to use the hovatek auto builder to build twrp and ofrp. They would build, but isn't working and in ofrp the hw navigation "vol keys + pwr" were being wonky. Later I generated my own device tree, but it wouldn't produce a recovery.img.

Adb works, fastboot works, and touch doesn't work, but the hw navigation works without issue.  It finds all the needed partitions, but I can't mount any of them

Not sure if I need to go the try and disable AVB/Verity and work on disabling FBE or try and get ofrp to work with it it's new territory for me. I'm fine with losing data for the millionth time. If anyone has any tips, I'm up for help or suggestions.

*Update*

Onto another tangent. If you install a dsu/gsi rom, and it happens to be android 16, there's a chance that it will break the permission controller on your stock rom.

To fix this, remove: "/metadata/aconfig/maps/system.flag.map" as it sets flags that are only needed on android 16.

>
>
>
> [View attachment 6309692](https://xdaforums.com/attachments/6309692/)
>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

AVB still verifies a bunch of partitions.

init_boot and recovery can be modified and it'll still boot.

Modifying boot seems to trigger AVB and forces a factory reset.

Attempting to disable vbmeta via fastboot commands, triggers a bootloader mode loop and requires and edl restore.

Changing normally protected settings with settings database editor causes the corrupt warning, but still boots.

Installing a dsu/gsi rom using root triggers the corrupt warning, but still boots.

Booting an android 16 rom adds files to /metadata that A15 doesn't like, and it crashes the permissions manager until they are deleted.

From what I understand, in simple terms ztecfg has to give permission to the eng-abl to allow unlocking. So the ztecfg partition is modified to allow the eng-abl, then it's signed and flashed. Followed by the eng-abl, which has all of the commands.

We can modify the zteconfig to match an unlocked device, but until the signing method is available to the public, it's useless.

---

### #391 — **bobbyp1086** · Feb 2, 2026 at 9:24 AM · page 20

And that can't be used to unlock bootloader? I had to rebuild my rm7 from a paperweight to booting using qfil. I know it can unlock bootloader. Or I'm missing something, anyhow I'm down to sacrifice this expensive turd in the name of unlocking all those who got duped like I did

### #392 — **DarkestSpawn** · Feb 2, 2026 at 1:00 PM · page 20

> **bobbyp1086 said:**
> And that can't be used to unlock bootloader? I had to rebuild my rm7 from a paperweight to booting using qfil. I know it can unlock bootloader. Or I'm missing something, anyhow I'm down to sacrifice this expensive turd in the name of unlocking all those who got duped like I did
>
>
> Click to expand...
>
> Click to collapse

Bootloader unlocking has been available for awhile. The problem is ztecfg partition needs to be pulled and signed and sent back for the bootloader to accept the eng_abl fastboot command unlock. What is not available to the public is the RSA algorithm used for signing atm. Without that, when you send the fastboot unlock command it will fail. That's what is being worked on behind the scenes, either cracking the RSA key (Not likely, or they get lucky and get the Algorithm used to sign so someone can make a program with it built in) or they figure out some CVE exploit bypassing Qualcomm bootloader and AVB (Which is more likely then cracking the RSA key, but still not easy) which will take time and possible hard bricks that folks don't want to chance (Most of these tests can be reversed with EDL but not all). There is also some possibilities via hardware (Pulling the back off and getting to certain test points/fuses, board swaps) tricks. All said, to my knowledge there are folks still going at it.

---

That's what is being worked on behind the scenes, either cracking the RSA key (Not likely, or they get lucky and get the Algorithm used to sign so someone can make a program with it built in) or they figure out some CVE exploit bypassing Qualcomm bootloader and AVB (Which is more likely then cracking the RSA key, but still not easy) which will take time and possible hard bricks that folks don't want to chance (Most of these tests can be reversed with EDL but not all). There is also some possibilities via hardware (Pulling the back off and getting to certain test points/fuses, board swaps) tricks. All said, to my knowledge there are folks still going at it.

### #423 — **BD_Security** · Feb 22, 2026 at 3:29 PM · page 22

Today I will be posting how to root REDMAGIC 10 Pro

KS want to work on this together?

### REDMAGIC 10 Pro - Complete EDL Recovery & Root Guide​
*Based on 26+ hours of debugging a bricked device*

### Table of Contents​

1. The Problem
2. Critical Discoveries
3. Prerequisites
4. Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode
5. Phase 2: Backup Partitions
6. Phase 3: Patch vbmeta
7. Phase 4: Root with Magisk
8. Complete Working Scripts
9. Troubleshooting
10. FAQ

### The Problem​

- Device stuck in **ZTE MemoryDump Mode** (VID_19D2![:p](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ID_0112)
- Phone displays: *"Your device is corrupt and will not boot"*
- Custom scripts fail with USB errors or programmer crashes
- Sahara upload works (38 chunks) but firehose never starts

### Critical Discoveries​

#### What DOESN'T Work ​

- **ZTE → SWITCH_MODE → 9008 transition** (corrupts USB state, kills programmer)
- clear_halt() after Sahara DONE (hangs 6-8 seconds, misses programmer window)
- Reconnecting to same handle after programmer starts (device disappears)
- Zero Length Packet (ZLP) after every chunk (corrupts data)
- Using 1,2,3,4,5,6 in HELLO_RESP reserved bytes (causes mode mismatch)

#### What DOES Work ​

1. **Clean 9008 entry** via volume buttons (bypass ZTE crash handler)
2. **Exact Sahara protocol** from edl_v5 (all-zero reserved bytes)
3. **NO post-DONE delays** - read immediately
4. **Continuous data + ONE ZLP** at the very end
5. **Flash BOTH** patched init_boot AND patched vbmeta
6. **Direct 9008 entry** = success. **ZTE transition** = failure.

#### The Real Insight ​
The programmer (devprg.melf) **IS** valid - it contains both XBL boot code AND firehose protocol strings (rawmode, configure, program, UFS). Sahara uploads 38 chunks successfully every time with DONE_RSP status=0.

The problem: After Sahara DONE, the programmer:

1. Restarts the USB controller
2. Re-enumerates as a NEW 9008 device (pkt=512 → pkt=1024)
3. Our old USB handle dies → Errno 19: No such device
4. Windows takes 60+ seconds to load drivers → programmer watchdog fires (8s) → crash → back to ZTE dump
**The "8-second window" is a myth.** We were always talking to a dead PBL handle, never the actual programmer.

### Prerequisites​

#### Hardware​

- REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
- USB-C cable (data capable)
- Windows PC (Linux/Mac can adapt)

#### Software​
powershell

# Python 3.8+ with:

pip install pyusb libusb

# bkerler-edl (optional but helpful)

git clone https://github.com/bkerler/edl

cd edl

pip install -r requirements.txt

# Stock files (backup BEFORE modifying):

- abl_b_dump.bin (from working device or extracted)

- devprg.melf (extracted from ZTE dump mode)

#### Files You'll Need​

FileSourceSizedevprg.melfExtracted via EDL/ZTE dump~1.6MBabl_b_dump.binBackup of stock abl_b1MBinit_boot_b.imgStock from device/firmware8MBvbmeta_b.imgStock from device/firmware64KB

### Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode​

#### The ONLY Reliable Method​
powershell

# 1. Unplug USB cable

# 2. Press and hold BOTH Volume Up + Volume Down

# 3. While holding buttons, plug USB cable back in

# 4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds

# 5. Device should appear as "Qualcomm HS-USB QDLoader 9008"

#### Verify Connection​
powershell

Get-PnpDevice | Where-Object { $_.InstanceId -match "VID_05C6.*PID_9008" }

# Should show: Status OK, FriendlyName contains "9008"

#### Why This Works​
This bypasses ZTE's crash handler entirely, putting the device in **PBL Sahara mode** with a clean USB state. The programmer will stay alive for ~8 seconds after loading.

### Phase 2: Backup Partitions​

#### Get Partition Layout​
From our working GPT dump, REDMAGIC 10 Pro LUN4 layout:

python

# Parse GPT (sector size 4096 bytes)

vbmeta_b        start=490260  sectors=16    size=65,536 bytes

init_boot_b     start=686048  sectors=2048  size=8,388,608 bytes

abl_b           start=448832  sectors=256   size=1,048,576 bytes

boot_b          start=683040  sectors=32768 size=134,217,728 bytes

#### Dump Critical Partitions​
Use this Python script while in 9008 mode:

python

# dump_partitions.py

import usb.core, usb.util, struct, time

def find_9008():

    dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)

    if not dev:

        print("No 9008 device found")

        return None

    return dev

def sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions):

    """Upload programmer and dump partitions via firehose"""

    # ... (see Complete Scripts section)

partitions = [

    ("vbmeta_b", 490260, 16, "vbmeta_b_stock.img"),

    ("init_boot_b", 686048, 2048, "init_boot_b_stock.img"),

    ("abl_b", 448832, 256, "abl_b_stock.img"),

]

dev = find_9008()

if dev:

    sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions)

### Phase 3: Patch vbmeta​

#### Why This is Critical​
Flashing a modified init_boot_b without disabling vbmeta verification will trigger AVB failure:

- **"Your device is corrupt"** screen
- Boot loop back to ZTE dump
- Rollback index mismatches

#### Manual vbmeta Patch​
python

def patch_vbmeta_flags(input_file, output_file):

    """Set AVB flags to 0x02 (verification disabled)"""

    with open(input_file, 'rb') as f:

        data = bytearray(f.read())

    # Flags are at offset 12 (0x0C), 4-byte little-endian

    # Change from 00 00 00 00 to 02 00 00 00

    data[12:16] = b'\x02\x00\x00\x00'

    with open(output_file, 'wb') as f:

        f.write(data)

    print(f"Patched {input_file} -> {output_file}")

patch_vbmeta_flags("vbmeta_b_stock.img", "vbmeta_b_patched.img")

#### Verify Patch​
bash

# Using avbtool (if available)

avbtool info_image --image vbmeta_b_patched.img | grep "Flags"

# Should show: Flags: 2

# Or hexdump

hexdump -C -n 64 vbmeta_b_patched.img | head

# At offset 0x0C: 02 00 00 00

### Phase 4: Root with Magisk​

#### Step 1: Patch init_boot with Magisk​
bash

# On phone (after booting)

# 1. Install Magisk APK

# 2. Copy stock init_boot_b.img to /sdcard/Download/

# 3. In Magisk app: Install → Select and Patch a File

# 4. Choose init_boot_b.img

# 5. Pull patched file: /sdcard/Download/magisk_patched.img

#### Step 2: Prepare Files for EDL Flash​
powershell

# Files needed in working directory:

- devprg.melf          # Programmer

- vbmeta_b_patched.img # Patched vbmeta (64KB)

- magisk_patched.img   # Patched init_boot (8MB)

#### Step 3: Flash Both Partitions​
Use the complete script below. **Critical**: Must flash in ONE EDL session with proper ZLP handling.

### Complete Working Scripts​

#### Script 1: Wait for Clean 9008​
python

# wait_9008.py

import usb.core, time

def wait_for_clean_9008(timeout=120):

    """

    Wait for device to enter clean 9008 mode via volume buttons.

    Returns USB device object or None.

    """

    print("=" * 60)

    print("CLEAN 9008 ENTRY INSTRUCTIONS:")

    print("1. UNPLUG USB cable")

    print("2. Press and hold BOTH VOLUME UP + VOLUME DOWN")

    print("3. While holding, PLUG USB CABLE BACK IN")

    print("4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds")

    print("=" * 60)

    print(f"\nWaiting up to {timeout} seconds for 9008 device...")

    start = time.time()

    while time.time() - start < timeout:

        dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)

        if dev:

            print(f"\n![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) 9008 FOUND! bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")

            return dev

        if int(time.time() - start) % 10 == 0:

            print(f"  {int(time.time() - start)}s...")

        time.sleep(1)

    print("\n![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found within timeout")

    return None

if __name__ == "__main__":

    dev = wait_for_clean_9008()

#### Script 2: Complete Flash (The One That Works)​
python

# root_redmagic.py

import usb.core, usb.util

import struct, time, os

# ========== CONFIGURATION ==========

LUN = 4

VBMETA_SECTOR = 490260

VBMETA_SECTORS = 16

INITBOOT_SECTOR = 686048

INITBOOT_SECTORS = 2048  # 8MB

PROG_FILE = "devprg.melf"

VBMETA_PATCHED = "vbmeta_b_patched.img"

INITBOOT_PATCHED = "magisk_patched.img"

# ========== USB SETUP ==========

def setup_usb(dev):

    """Configure USB endpoints for Sahara/firehose"""

    try:

        if dev.is_kernel_driver_active(0):

            dev.detach_kernel_driver(0)

    except:

        pass

    try:

        dev.set_configuration()

    except:

        pass

    cfg = dev.get_active_configuration()

    intf = cfg[(0,0)]

    ep_out = usb.util.find_descriptor(

        intf,

        custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_OUT

    )

    ep_in = usb.util.find_descriptor(

        intf,

        custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_IN

    )

    return ep_out, ep_in

def read_ep(ep, timeout=2000, size=4096):

    """Safely read from endpoint"""

    try:

        return bytes(ep.read(size, timeout=timeout))

    except:

        return b''

def write_ep(ep, data, timeout=5000):

    """Safely write to endpoint"""

    if isinstance(data, str):

        data = data.encode()

    try:

        ep.write(data, timeout=timeout)

        return True

    except Exception as e:

        print(f"  WRITE ERROR: {e}")

        return False

# ========== SAHARA PROTOCOL ==========

def sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):

    """

    Upload programmer via Sahara.

    Returns True if successful (38 chunks, DONE_RSP received)

    """

    print("\n=== SAHARA UPLOAD ===")

    # Read HELLO

    hello = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000, size=256)

    if not hello or len(hello) < 24:

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No Sahara HELLO received")

        return False

    cmd = struct.unpack('<I', hello[0:4])[0]

    if cmd != 0x01:

        print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Not HELLO: cmd=0x{cmd:x}")

        return False

    ver = struct.unpack('<I', hello[8:12])[0]

    verc = struct.unpack('<I', hello[12:16])[0]

    mode = struct.unpack('<I', hello[20:24])[0]

    print(f"HELLO: v{ver}/{verc} mode={mode}")

    # Send HELLO_RESP (ALL ZEROS - CRITICAL!)

    resp = struct.pack('<IIIIIIIIIIII',

                       0x02, 0x30, ver, verc,

                       0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)

    if not write_ep(ep_out, resp):

        return False

    # Upload loop

    chunks = 0

    while True:

        pkt = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)

        if not pkt:

            print("![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Timeout waiting for command")

            break

        cmd = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[0:4])[0]

        if cmd == 0x12:  # READ_DATA_64

            off = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[16:24])[0]

            ln = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[24:32])[0]

            if chunks == 0:

                print(f"First READ_DATA_64: off={off} len={ln}")

            write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))

            chunks += 1

        elif cmd == 0x03:  # READ_DATA

            off = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]

            ln = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[16:20])[0]

            write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))

            chunks += 1

        elif cmd == 0x04:  # END_TRANSFER

            status = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]

            print(f"END_TRANSFER: status={status} chunks={chunks}")

            # Send DONE_REQ

            write_ep(ep_out, struct.pack('<II', 0x05, 0x08))

            # Read DONE_RSP

            done = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)

            if done:

                done_cmd = struct.unpack('<I', done[0:4])[0]

                print(f"DONE_RSP: cmd=0x{done_cmd:x}")

            break

        else:

            print(f"![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Unknown command: 0x{cmd:x}")

            break

    success = (chunks == 38)  # Known good count for devprg.melf

    print(f"Sahara {'![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) SUCCESS' if success else '![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) FAILED'} ({chunks} chunks)")

    return success

# ========== FIREHOSE PROTOCOL ==========

def firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):

    """Send configure XML and wait for ACK"""

    print("\n=== CONFIGURING FIREHOSE ===")

    cfg_xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?><data><configure MemoryName="UFS" Verbose="0" AlwaysValidate="0" MaxDigestTableSizeInBytes="2048" MaxPayloadSizeToTargetInBytes="1048576" ZLPAwareHost="1" SkipStorageInit="0" SkipWrite="0" Oem="ZTE"/></data>'

    if not write_ep(ep_out, cfg_xml):

        return False

    # Wait for ACK (up to 10s)

    for i in range(20):

        resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=1000)

        if resp:

            txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')

            print(f"  {txt[:150]}")

            if 'value="ACK"' in txt:

                print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Configure ACK received")

                return True

            if 'value="NAK"' in txt:

                print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Configure NAK")

                return False

        time.sleep(0.5)

    print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No configure response")

    return False

def firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, data, start_sector, num_sectors, name):

    """

    Flash data to partition.

    CRITICAL: Send ALL data, then ONE ZLP at the end

    """

    print(f"\n=== PROGRAMMING {name} ===")

    print(f"Start sector: {start_sector}, Sectors: {num_sectors}, Size: {len(data)} bytes")

    # Send program command

    prog_xml = f'<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><program SECTOR_SIZE_IN_BYTES="4096" num_partition_sectors="{num_sectors}" physical_partition_number="{LUN}" start_sector="{start_sector}" filename="{name}"/></data>'

    if not write_ep(ep_out, prog_xml):

        return False

    # Wait for rawmode ACK

    rawmode = False

    for i in range(30):

        resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000)

        if resp:

            txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')

            print(f"  {txt[:150]}")

            if 'rawmode="true"' in txt.lower() and 'value="ACK"' in txt:

                rawmode = True

                break

            if 'value="NAK"' in txt:

                print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Program NAK")

                return False

        time.sleep(0.2)

    if not rawmode:

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No rawmode ACK")

        return False

    print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Rawmode ACK received, sending data...")

    # Send ALL data continuously

    sent = 0

    chunk_size = 65536  # 64KB chunks for USB

    while sent < len(data):

        end = min(sent + chunk_size, len(data))

        if not write_ep(ep_out, data[sent:end], timeout=30000):

            print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Write failed at {sent}/{len(data)}")

            return False

        sent = end

        if sent % 262144 == 0 or sent == len(data):

            print(f"  Sent {sent}/{len(data)} bytes")

    # CRITICAL: Send Zero Length Packet at the very end

    print("Sending ZLP...")

    write_ep(ep_out, b"", timeout=1000)

    # Wait for final ACK

    print("Waiting for flash ACK...")

    for i in range(60):

        resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000)

        if resp:

            txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')

            print(f"  {txt[:200]}")

            if 'value="ACK"' in txt:

                print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) {name} flashed successfully!")

                return True

            if 'value="NAK"' in txt:

                print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) {name} flash NAK")

                return False

        time.sleep(0.5)

    print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No final ACK for {name}")

    return False

# ========== MAIN ==========

def main():

    print("=" * 70)

    print("REDMAGIC 10 Pro - EDL Root Script")

    print("=" * 70)

    # Wait for clean 9008

    print("\n[1/5] Waiting for clean 9008 mode...")

    print("Follow instructions above, then press Enter when ready")

    input()

    dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)

    if not dev:

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found")

        return

    print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Found 9008: bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")

    # Setup USB

    print("\n[2/5] Setting up USB...")

    ep_out, ep_in = setup_usb(dev)

    print(f"Endpoints: OUT=0x{ep_out.bEndpointAddress:x} IN=0x{ep_in.bEndpointAddress:x}")

    print(f"Max packet: {ep_in.wMaxPacketSize}")

    # Load programmer

    print("\n[3/5] Loading programmer...")

    with open(PROG_FILE, 'rb') as f:

        prog_data = f.read()

    print(f"Programmer size: {len(prog_data)} bytes")

    if not sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Sahara upload failed")

        return

    # Wait for programmer to start

    print("\nWaiting 2 seconds for programmer to initialize...")

    time.sleep(2)

    # Configure firehose

    if not firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Firehose configure failed")

        return

    # Load patched vbmeta

    print("\n[4/5] Loading patched vbmeta...")

    with open(VBMETA_PATCHED, 'rb') as f:

        vbmeta_data = f.read()

    print(f"vbmeta_b size: {len(vbmeta_data)} bytes (should be 65536)")

    # Flash vbmeta_b

    if not firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, vbmeta_data, VBMETA_SECTOR, VBMETA_SECTORS, "vbmeta_b"):

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) vbmeta_b flash failed")

        return

    # Load patched init_boot

    print("\n[5/5] Loading patched init_boot...")

    with open(INITBOOT_PATCHED, 'rb') as f:

        init_data = f.read()

    print(f"init_boot_b size: {len(init_data)} bytes (should be 8388608)")

    # Flash init_boot_b

    if not firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, init_data, INITBOOT_SECTOR, INITBOOT_SECTORS, "init_boot_b"):

        print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) init_boot_b flash failed")

        return

    # Success!

    print("\n" + "=" * 70)

    print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) ROOT SUCCESSFUL! ![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)")

    print("=" * 70)

    print("\nSending reboot command...")

    # Reboot

    write_ep(ep_out, '<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><power value="reset"/></data>')

    time.sleep(1)

    print("\nPhone should now boot with Magisk installed!")

    print("First boot may take 2-3 minutes.")

if __name__ == "__main__":

    main()

### Troubleshooting​

#### "No 9008 device found"​
**Problem:** Volume button method didn't work

**Solution:**

powershell

# Try these alternatives:

1. Let battery die completely, then try volume buttons

2. From fastboot: fastboot reboot edl

3. From ADB (if bootable): adb reboot edl

4. Use EDL test point (last resort - requires opening phone)

#### Sahara upload fails (not 38 chunks)​
**Problem:** Wrong programmer or corrupted file

**Solution:**

powershell

# Verify devprg.melf is correct

python -c "

data = open('devprg.melf','rb').read()

print('Size:', len(data))

print('ELF magic:', data[:4])

print('Has firehose strings:', b'configure' in data)

"

# Should show: Size ~1.6MB, b'configure' found

#### Configure NAK / No response​
**Problem:** Programmer not starting firehose mode

**Solution:**

- Ensure you entered **clean 9008** (volume buttons), NOT ZTE→9008
- Try waiting 3 seconds after Sahara instead of 2
- Check if USB reset happened (device should briefly disappear)

#### Flash succeeds but phone won't boot​
**Problem:** AVB still active or wrong partition

**Solution:**

python

# Verify vbmeta patch

with open('vbmeta_b_patched.img','rb') as f:

    data = f.read()

print(f"Flags at offset 12: {data[12:16].hex()}")

# Should show: 02000000

#### Phone stuck at "Your device is corrupt"​
**Problem:** vbmeta verification still enabled

**Solution:**

- Re-flash with proper vbmeta patch (flags=2)
- Check if you flashed to correct slot (make sure it's _b)
- Consider flashing both slots if unsure

#### Windows can't find device after Sahara​
**Problem:** USB re-enumeration timing

**Solution:**

- Use the script above - it reconnects properly
- Don't use Zadig or change drivers - libusb backend works
- If using Zadig, install WinUSB for 9008 mode

### FAQ​

#### Q: Is devprg.melf the correct programmer?​
**A:** Yes! It contains firehose protocol strings (configure, rawmode, program, UFS). The issue was never the programmer - it was USB re-enumeration.

#### Q: Why doesn't ZTE → SWITCH_MODE work?​
**A:** The ZTE crash handler leaves USB in a dirty state. After transition, the programmer's USB reset creates a new device that Windows takes 60+ seconds to enumerate - by then the programmer has crashed (8s watchdog).

#### Q: What's with the Zero Length Packet (ZLP)?​
**A:** Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" expects a ZLP after data transfers that are exact multiples of USB packet size. 8MB (8388608 bytes) is a multiple of 512/1024, so a ZLP is required. Sending ZLP after every chunk corrupts the data.

#### Q: Do I need to flash both slots?​
**A:** For safety, flash only slot B if that's your active slot. Check with:

bash

# In fastboot

fastboot getvar current-slot

If unsure, you can flash both - just adjust sector addresses from GPT.

#### Q: What about other vbmeta partitions (system, vendor)?​
**A:** The main vbmeta controls boot image verification. If you're only modifying init_boot, patching main vbmeta is sufficient. If you modify system/vendor later, you'll need to patch those too.

#### Q: Will this work on other REDMAGIC models?​
**A:** The principles apply, but partition addresses will differ. You'll need to dump GPT from your specific model first.

#### Q: My phone won't enter 9008 at all!​
**A:** Last resort - EDL test point. Requires opening the phone and shorting specific pads. Check XDA for your model's test point location.

#### Q: Is the bootloader unlocked after this?​
**A:** No - this method bypasses the bootloader entirely via EDL. The bootloader remains locked. You're rooted with a locked bootloader, which is possible on Qualcomm devices via EDL.

### Partition Reference (REDMAGIC 10 Pro - NX789J)​

#### LUN4 GPT (User Data/System Partitions)​
text

Partition           Start Sector    Sectors     Size

------------------  -------------   --------    --------

xbl_b               184             15360       60MB

abl_b               448832          256         1MB

boot_b              683040          32768       128MB

init_boot_b         686048          2048        8MB

vbmeta_b            490260          16          64KB

vbmeta_system_b     520120          16          64KB

vbmeta_vendor_b     492584          16          64KB

#### Critical Addresses for Rooting​
python

VBMETA_B = {

    'lun': 4,

    'start': 490260,

    'sectors': 16,

    'size': 65536

}

INIT_BOOT_B = {

    'lun': 4,

    'start': 686048,

    'sectors': 2048,

    'size': 8388608

}

**The most important lesson:** Don't trust the 8-second window. The programmer is alive for ~8 seconds, but you have to catch it in the first 2 seconds after USB re-enumeration. The volume button method gives you a clean state where the programmer stays alive and the USB handle remains valid.

**The ZLP (Zero Length Packet) issue** cost us 10+ hours. Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" is strict about protocol - one ZLP at the end, not after every chunk.

**vbmeta is NOT optional** - if you flash a modified init_boot without patching vbmeta, you'll get "device is corrupt" every time. Patch flags to 0x02.

**The programmer IS correct** - devprg.melf from ZTE dump mode is a valid firehose programmer. Don't waste time searching for another one.

*This guide represents 26+ hours of debugging across 50+ scripts, 3 USB protocol analyzers, and 2 near-brick scares. I will share freely on XDA and help others avoid the same pitfalls.*

**Last Updated:** February 2025

**Device:** REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)

**Android Version:** 15

**Kernel:** GKI compatible

> **BD_Security said:**
> ### REDMAGIC 10 Pro - Complete EDL Recovery & Root Guide​
> *Based on 26+ hours of debugging a bricked device*
>

>

>
> 1. The Problem
> 2. Critical Discoveries
> 3. Prerequisites

>
> ### The Problem​
>
> - Device stuck in **ZTE MemoryDump Mode** (VID_19D2![:p](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ID_0112)
> - Phone displays: *"Your device is corrupt and will not boot"*
> - Custom scripts fail with USB errors or programmer crashes
> - Sahara upload works (38 chunks) but firehose never starts
>
> ### Critical Discoveries​
>
> #### What DOESN'T Work ​
>
> - **ZTE → SWITCH_MODE → 9008 transition** (corrupts USB state, kills programmer)
> - clear_halt() after Sahara DONE (hangs 6-8 seconds, misses programmer window)
> - Reconnecting to same handle after programmer starts (device disappears)
> - Zero Length Packet (ZLP) after every chunk (corrupts data)
> - Using 1,2,3,4,5,6 in HELLO_RESP reserved bytes (causes mode mismatch)
>
> #### What DOES Work ​
>
> 1. **Clean 9008 entry** via volume buttons (bypass ZTE crash handler)
> 2. **Exact Sahara protocol** from edl_v5 (all-zero reserved bytes)
> 3. **NO post-DONE delays** - read immediately
> 4. **Continuous data + ONE ZLP** at the very end
> 5. **Flash BOTH** patched init_boot AND patched vbmeta
> 6. **Direct 9008 entry** = success. **ZTE transition** = failure.
>
> #### The Real Insight ​
> The programmer (devprg.melf) **IS** valid - it contains both XBL boot code AND firehose protocol strings (rawmode, configure, program, UFS). Sahara uploads 38 chunks successfully every time with DONE_RSP status=0.
>
>
>
> The problem: After Sahara DONE, the programmer:
>
>
>
>
> 1. Restarts the USB controller
> 2. Re-enumerates as a NEW 9008 device (pkt=512 → pkt=1024)
> 3. Our old USB handle dies → Errno 19: No such device
> 4. Windows takes 60+ seconds to load drivers → programmer watchdog fires (8s) → crash → back to ZTE dump
> **The "8-second window" is a myth.** We were always talking to a dead PBL handle, never the actual programmer.
>
>
>
>
>
>

> ### Phase 3: Patch vbmeta​
>
> #### Why This is Critical​
> Flashing a modified init_boot_b without disabling vbmeta verification will trigger AVB failure:
>
>
>
>
> - **"Your device is corrupt"** screen
> - Boot loop back to ZTE dump
> - Rollback index mismatches
>
> #### Manual vbmeta Patch​
> python
>
> def patch_vbmeta_flags(input_file, output_file):
>
>     """Set AVB flags to 0x02 (verification disabled)"""
>
>     with open(input_file, 'rb') as f:
>
>         data = bytearray(f.read())
>
>
>
>     # Flags are at offset 12 (0x0C), 4-byte little-endian
>
>     # Change from 00 00 00 00 to 02 00 00 00
>
>     data[12:16] = b'\x02\x00\x00\x00'
>
>
>
>     with open(output_file, 'wb') as f:
>
>         f.write(data)
>
>     print(f"Patched {input_file} -> {output_file}")
>
>
>
> patch_vbmeta_flags("vbmeta_b_stock.img", "vbmeta_b_patched.img")
>
>
> #### Verify Patch​
> bash
>
> # Using avbtool (if available)
>
> avbtool info_image --image vbmeta_b_patched.img | grep "Flags"
>
> # Should show: Flags: 2
>
>
>
> # Or hexdump
>
> hexdump -C -n 64 vbmeta_b_patched.img | head
>
> # At offset 0x0C: 02 00 00 00
>
>
>
>

> # 3. In Magisk app: Install → Select and Patch a File

> # 4. Choose init_boot_b.img
>
> # 5. Pull patched file: /sdcard/Download/magisk_patched.img
>
>

> powershell
>
> # Files needed in working directory:
>
> - devprg.melf          # Programmer
>
> - vbmeta_b_patched.img # Patched vbmeta (64KB)
>
> - magisk_patched.img   # Patched init_boot (8MB)

> #### Step 3: Flash Both Partitions​
> Use the complete script below. **Critical**: Must flash in ONE EDL session with proper ZLP handling.
>

> ### Complete Working Scripts​
>
> #### Script 1: Wait for Clean 9008​
> python
>
> # wait_9008.py
>
> import usb.core, time
>
>
>
> def wait_for_clean_9008(timeout=120):
>
>     """
>
>     Wait for device to enter clean 9008 mode via volume buttons.
>
>     Returns USB device object or None.
>
>     """
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print("CLEAN 9008 ENTRY INSTRUCTIONS:")
>
>     print("1. UNPLUG USB cable")
>
>     print("2. Press and hold BOTH VOLUME UP + VOLUME DOWN")
>
>     print("3. While holding, PLUG USB CABLE BACK IN")
>
>     print("4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds")
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print(f"\nWaiting up to {timeout} seconds for 9008 device...")
>
>
>
>     start = time.time()
>
>     while time.time() - start < timeout:
>
>         dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>         if dev:
>
>             print(f"\n![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) 9008 FOUND! bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")
>
>             return dev
>
>         if int(time.time() - start) % 10 == 0:
>
>             print(f"  {int(time.time() - start)}s...")
>
>         time.sleep(1)
>
>
>
>     print("\n![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found within timeout")
>
>     return None
>
>
>
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>
>     dev = wait_for_clean_9008()
>
>
> #### Script 2: Complete Flash (The One That Works)​
> python
>
> # root_redmagic.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util
>
> import struct, time, os
>
>
>
> # ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
>
> LUN = 4
>
> VBMETA_SECTOR = 490260
>
> VBMETA_SECTORS = 16
>
> INITBOOT_SECTOR = 686048
>
> INITBOOT_SECTORS = 2048  # 8MB
>
>
>
> PROG_FILE = "devprg.melf"
>
> VBMETA_PATCHED = "vbmeta_b_patched.img"
>
> INITBOOT_PATCHED = "magisk_patched.img"
>
>
>
> # ========== USB SETUP ==========
>
> def setup_usb(dev):
>
>     """Configure USB endpoints for Sahara/firehose"""
>
>     try:
>
>         if dev.is_kernel_driver_active(0):
>
>             dev.detach_kernel_driver(0)
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     try:
>
>         dev.set_configuration()
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     cfg = dev.get_active_configuration()
>
>     intf = cfg[(0,0)]
>
>
>
>     ep_out = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_OUT
>
>     )
>
>     ep_in = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_IN
>
>     )
>
>
>
>     return ep_out, ep_in
>
>
>
> def read_ep(ep, timeout=2000, size=4096):
>
>     """Safely read from endpoint"""
>
>     try:
>
>         return bytes(ep.read(size, timeout=timeout))
>
>     except:
>
>         return b''
>
>
>
> def write_ep(ep, data, timeout=5000):
>
>     """Safely write to endpoint"""
>
>     if isinstance(data, str):
>
>         data = data.encode()
>
>     try:
>
>         ep.write(data, timeout=timeout)
>
>         return True
>
>     except Exception as e:
>
>         print(f"  WRITE ERROR: {e}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
> # ========== SAHARA PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):
>
>     """
>
>     Upload programmer via Sahara.
>
>     Returns True if successful (38 chunks, DONE_RSP received)
>
>     """
>
>     print("\n=== SAHARA UPLOAD ===")
>
>
>
>     # Read HELLO
>
>     hello = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000, size=256)
>
>     if not hello or len(hello) < 24:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No Sahara HELLO received")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     cmd = struct.unpack('<I', hello[0:4])[0]
>
>     if cmd != 0x01:
>
>         print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Not HELLO: cmd=0x{cmd:x}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     ver = struct.unpack('<I', hello[8:12])[0]
>
>     verc = struct.unpack('<I', hello[12:16])[0]
>
>     mode = struct.unpack('<I', hello[20:24])[0]
>
>     print(f"HELLO: v{ver}/{verc} mode={mode}")
>
>
>
>     # Send HELLO_RESP (ALL ZEROS - CRITICAL!)
>
>     resp = struct.pack('<IIIIIIIIIIII',
>
>                        0x02, 0x30, ver, verc,
>
>                        0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, resp):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Upload loop
>
>     chunks = 0
>
>     while True:
>
>         pkt = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>         if not pkt:
>
>             print("![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Timeout waiting for command")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         cmd = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[0:4])[0]
>
>
>
>         if cmd == 0x12:  # READ_DATA_64
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[16:24])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[24:32])[0]
>
>             if chunks == 0:
>
>                 print(f"First READ_DATA_64: off={off} len={ln}")
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x03:  # READ_DATA
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[16:20])[0]
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x04:  # END_TRANSFER
>
>             status = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             print(f"END_TRANSFER: status={status} chunks={chunks}")
>
>
>
>             # Send DONE_REQ
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, struct.pack('<II', 0x05, 0x08))
>
>
>
>             # Read DONE_RSP
>
>             done = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>             if done:
>
>                 done_cmd = struct.unpack('<I', done[0:4])[0]
>
>                 print(f"DONE_RSP: cmd=0x{done_cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         else:
>
>             print(f"![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Unknown command: 0x{cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>     success = (chunks == 38)  # Known good count for devprg.melf
>
>     print(f"Sahara {'![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) SUCCESS' if success else '![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) FAILED'} ({chunks} chunks)")
>
>     return success
>
>
>
> # ========== FIREHOSE PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):
>
>     """Send configure XML and wait for ACK"""
>
>     print("\n=== CONFIGURING FIREHOSE ===")
>
>
>
>     cfg_xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?><data><configure MemoryName="UFS" Verbose="0" AlwaysValidate="0" MaxDigestTableSizeInBytes="2048" MaxPayloadSizeToTargetInBytes="1048576" ZLPAwareHost="1" SkipStorageInit="0" SkipWrite="0" Oem="ZTE"/></data>'
>
>
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, cfg_xml):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Wait for ACK (up to 10s)
>
>     for i in range(20):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=1000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Configure ACK received")
>
>                 return True
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Configure NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.5)
>
>
>
>     print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No configure response")
>
>     return False
>
>
>
> def firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, data, start_sector, num_sectors, name):
>
>     """
>
>     Flash data to partition.
>
>     CRITICAL: Send ALL data, then ONE ZLP at the end
>
>     """
>
>     print(f"\n=== PROGRAMMING {name} ===")
>
>     print(f"Start sector: {start_sector}, Sectors: {num_sectors}, Size: {len(data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     # Send program command
>
>     prog_xml = f'<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><program SECTOR_SIZE_IN_BYTES="4096" num_partition_sectors="{num_sectors}" physical_partition_number="{LUN}" start_sector="{start_sector}" filename="{name}"/></data>'
>
>
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, prog_xml):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Wait for rawmode ACK
>
>     rawmode = False
>
>     for i in range(30):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'rawmode="true"' in txt.lower() and 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 rawmode = True
>
>                 break
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Program NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.2)
>
>
>
>     if not rawmode:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No rawmode ACK")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Rawmode ACK received, sending data...")
>
>
>
>     # Send ALL data continuously
>
>     sent = 0
>
>     chunk_size = 65536  # 64KB chunks for USB
>
>     while sent < len(data):
>
>         end = min(sent + chunk_size, len(data))
>
>         if not write_ep(ep_out, data[sent:end], timeout=30000):
>
>             print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Write failed at {sent}/{len(data)}")
>
>             return False
>
>         sent = end
>
>         if sent % 262144 == 0 or sent == len(data):
>
>             print(f"  Sent {sent}/{len(data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     # CRITICAL: Send Zero Length Packet at the very end
>
>     print("Sending ZLP...")
>
>     write_ep(ep_out, b"", timeout=1000)
>
>
>
>     # Wait for final ACK
>
>     print("Waiting for flash ACK...")
>
>     for i in range(60):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:200]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) {name} flashed successfully!")
>
>                 return True
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) {name} flash NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.5)
>
>
>
>     print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No final ACK for {name}")
>
>     return False
>
>
>
> # ========== MAIN ==========
>
> def main():
>
>     print("=" * 70)
>
>     print("REDMAGIC 10 Pro - EDL Root Script")
>
>     print("=" * 70)
>
>
>
>     # Wait for clean 9008
>
>     print("\n[1/5] Waiting for clean 9008 mode...")
>
>     print("Follow instructions above, then press Enter when ready")
>
>     input()
>
>
>
>     dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>     if not dev:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Found 9008: bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")
>
>
>
>     # Setup USB
>
>     print("\n[2/5] Setting up USB...")
>
>     ep_out, ep_in = setup_usb(dev)
>
>     print(f"Endpoints: OUT=0x{ep_out.bEndpointAddress:x} IN=0x{ep_in.bEndpointAddress:x}")
>
>     print(f"Max packet: {ep_in.wMaxPacketSize}")
>
>
>
>     # Load programmer
>
>     print("\n[3/5] Loading programmer...")
>
>     with open(PROG_FILE, 'rb') as f:
>
>         prog_data = f.read()
>
>     print(f"Programmer size: {len(prog_data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     if not sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Sahara upload failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Wait for programmer to start
>
>     print("\nWaiting 2 seconds for programmer to initialize...")
>
>     time.sleep(2)
>
>
>
>     # Configure firehose
>
>     if not firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Firehose configure failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Load patched vbmeta
>
>     print("\n[4/5] Loading patched vbmeta...")
>
>     with open(VBMETA_PATCHED, 'rb') as f:
>
>         vbmeta_data = f.read()
>
>     print(f"vbmeta_b size: {len(vbmeta_data)} bytes (should be 65536)")
>
>
>
>     # Flash vbmeta_b
>
>     if not firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, vbmeta_data, VBMETA_SECTOR, VBMETA_SECTORS, "vbmeta_b"):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) vbmeta_b flash failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Load patched init_boot
>
>     print("\n[5/5] Loading patched init_boot...")
>
>     with open(INITBOOT_PATCHED, 'rb') as f:
>
>         init_data = f.read()
>
>     print(f"init_boot_b size: {len(init_data)} bytes (should be 8388608)")
>
>
>
>     # Flash init_boot_b
>
>     if not firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, init_data, INITBOOT_SECTOR, INITBOOT_SECTORS, "init_boot_b"):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) init_boot_b flash failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Success!
>
>     print("\n" + "=" * 70)
>
>     print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) ROOT SUCCESSFUL! ![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)")
>
>     print("=" * 70)
>
>     print("\nSending reboot command...")
>
>
>
>     # Reboot
>
>     write_ep(ep_out, '<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><power value="reset"/></data>')
>
>     time.sleep(1)
>
>
>
>     print("\nPhone should now boot with Magisk installed!")
>
>     print("First boot may take 2-3 minutes.")
>
>
>
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>
>     main()

> ### Troubleshooting​
>
> #### "No 9008 device found"​
> **Problem:** Volume button method didn't work
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Try these alternatives:
>
> 1. Let battery die completely, then try volume buttons
>
> 2. From fastboot: fastboot reboot edl
>
> 3. From ADB (if bootable): adb reboot edl
>
> 4. Use EDL test point (last resort - requires opening phone)
>
>
> #### Sahara upload fails (not 38 chunks)​
> **Problem:** Wrong programmer or corrupted file
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Verify devprg.melf is correct
>
> python -c "
>
> data = open('devprg.melf','rb').read()
>
> print('Size:', len(data))
>
> print('ELF magic:', data[:4])
>
> print('Has firehose strings:', b'configure' in data)
>
> "
>
> # Should show: Size ~1.6MB, b'configure' found
>
>
> #### Configure NAK / No response​
> **Problem:** Programmer not starting firehose mode
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Ensure you entered **clean 9008** (volume buttons), NOT ZTE→9008
> - Try waiting 3 seconds after Sahara instead of 2
> - Check if USB reset happened (device should briefly disappear)
>
> #### Flash succeeds but phone won't boot​
> **Problem:** AVB still active or wrong partition
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Verify vbmeta patch
>
> with open('vbmeta_b_patched.img','rb') as f:
>
>     data = f.read()
>
> print(f"Flags at offset 12: {data[12:16].hex()}")
>
> # Should show: 02000000
>
>
> #### Phone stuck at "Your device is corrupt"​
> **Problem:** vbmeta verification still enabled
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Re-flash with proper vbmeta patch (flags=2)
> - Check if you flashed to correct slot (make sure it's _b)
> - Consider flashing both slots if unsure
>
> #### Windows can't find device after Sahara​
> **Problem:** USB re-enumeration timing
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Use the script above - it reconnects properly
> - Don't use Zadig or change drivers - libusb backend works
> - If using Zadig, install WinUSB for 9008 mode
>
>
>
> ### FAQ​
>
> #### Q: Is devprg.melf the correct programmer?​
> **A:** Yes! It contains firehose protocol strings (configure, rawmode, program, UFS). The issue was never the programmer - it was USB re-enumeration.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Why doesn't ZTE → SWITCH_MODE work?​
> **A:** The ZTE crash handler leaves USB in a dirty state. After transition, the programmer's USB reset creates a new device that Windows takes 60+ seconds to enumerate - by then the programmer has crashed (8s watchdog).
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What's with the Zero Length Packet (ZLP)?​
> **A:** Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" expects a ZLP after data transfers that are exact multiples of USB packet size. 8MB (8388608 bytes) is a multiple of 512/1024, so a ZLP is required. Sending ZLP after every chunk corrupts the data.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Do I need to flash both slots?​
> **A:** For safety, flash only slot B if that's your active slot. Check with:
>
>
>
> bash
>
> # In fastboot
>
> fastboot getvar current-slot
>
> If unsure, you can flash both - just adjust sector addresses from GPT.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What about other vbmeta partitions (system, vendor)?​
> **A:** The main vbmeta controls boot image verification. If you're only modifying init_boot, patching main vbmeta is sufficient. If you modify system/vendor later, you'll need to patch those too.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Will this work on other REDMAGIC models?​
> **A:** The principles apply, but partition addresses will differ. You'll need to dump GPT from your specific model first.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: My phone won't enter 9008 at all!​
> **A:** Last resort - EDL test point. Requires opening the phone and shorting specific pads. Check XDA for your model's test point location.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Is the bootloader unlocked after this?​
> **A:** No - this method bypasses the bootloader entirely via EDL. The bootloader remains locked. You're rooted with a locked bootloader, which is possible on Qualcomm devices via EDL.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Partition Reference (REDMAGIC 10 Pro - NX789J)​
>
> #### LUN4 GPT (User Data/System Partitions)​
> text
>
> Partition           Start Sector    Sectors     Size
>
> ------------------  -------------   --------    --------
>
> xbl_b               184             15360       60MB
>
> abl_b               448832          256         1MB
>
> boot_b              683040          32768       128MB
>
> init_boot_b         686048          2048        8MB
>
> vbmeta_b            490260          16          64KB
>
> vbmeta_system_b     520120          16          64KB
>
> vbmeta_vendor_b     492584          16          64KB
>
>
> #### Critical Addresses for Rooting​
> python
>
> VBMETA_B = {
>
>     'lun': 4,
>
>     'start': 490260,
>
>     'sectors': 16,
>
>     'size': 65536
>
> }
>
>
>
> INIT_BOOT_B = {
>
>     'lun': 4,
>
>     'start': 686048,
>
>     'sectors': 2048,
>
>     'size': 8388608
>
> }
>
>
>
> **The most important lesson:** Don't trust the 8-second window. The programmer is alive for ~8 seconds, but you have to catch it in the first 2 seconds after USB re-enumeration. The volume button method gives you a clean state where the programmer stays alive and the USB handle remains valid.
>
>
>
> **The ZLP (Zero Length Packet) issue** cost us 10+ hours. Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" is strict about protocol - one ZLP at the end, not after every chunk.
>
>
>
> **vbmeta is NOT optional** - if you flash a modified init_boot without patching vbmeta, you'll get "device is corrupt" every time. Patch flags to 0x02.
>
>
>
> **The programmer IS correct** - devprg.melf from ZTE dump mode is a valid firehose programmer. Don't waste time searching for another one.
>
>
>
>
>
> *This guide represents 26+ hours of debugging across 50+ scripts, 3 USB protocol analyzers, and 2 near-brick scares. I will share freely on XDA and help others avoid the same pitfalls.*
>
>
>
> **Last Updated:** February 2025
>
> **Device:** REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
>
> **Android Version:** 15
>
> **Kernel:** GKI compatible

### #425 — **Nicot38** · Feb 22, 2026 at 10:35 PM · page 22

> **BD_Security said:**
> ### REDMAGIC 10 Pro - Complete EDL Recovery & Root Guide​
> *Based on 26+ hours of debugging a bricked device*
>
>
>
>
> ### Table of Contents​
>
> 1. The Problem
> 2. Critical Discoveries
> 3. Prerequisites
> 4. Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode
> 5. Phase 2: Backup Partitions
> 6. Phase 3: Patch vbmeta
> 7. Phase 4: Root with Magisk
> 8. Complete Working Scripts
> 9. Troubleshooting
> 10. FAQ
>
>
>
> ### The Problem​
>
> - Device stuck in **ZTE MemoryDump Mode** (VID_19D2![:p](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ID_0112)
> - Phone displays: *"Your device is corrupt and will not boot"*
> - Custom scripts fail with USB errors or programmer crashes
> - Sahara upload works (38 chunks) but firehose never starts
>
> ### Critical Discoveries​
>
> #### What DOESN'T Work ​
>
> - **ZTE → SWITCH_MODE → 9008 transition** (corrupts USB state, kills programmer)
> - clear_halt() after Sahara DONE (hangs 6-8 seconds, misses programmer window)
> - Reconnecting to same handle after programmer starts (device disappears)
> - Zero Length Packet (ZLP) after every chunk (corrupts data)
> - Using 1,2,3,4,5,6 in HELLO_RESP reserved bytes (causes mode mismatch)
>
> #### What DOES Work ​
>
> 1. **Clean 9008 entry** via volume buttons (bypass ZTE crash handler)
> 2. **Exact Sahara protocol** from edl_v5 (all-zero reserved bytes)
> 3. **NO post-DONE delays** - read immediately
> 4. **Continuous data + ONE ZLP** at the very end
> 5. **Flash BOTH** patched init_boot AND patched vbmeta
> 6. **Direct 9008 entry** = success. **ZTE transition** = failure.
>
> #### The Real Insight ​
> The programmer (devprg.melf) **IS** valid - it contains both XBL boot code AND firehose protocol strings (rawmode, configure, program, UFS). Sahara uploads 38 chunks successfully every time with DONE_RSP status=0.
>
>
>
> The problem: After Sahara DONE, the programmer:
>
>
>
>
> 1. Restarts the USB controller
> 2. Re-enumerates as a NEW 9008 device (pkt=512 → pkt=1024)
> 3. Our old USB handle dies → Errno 19: No such device
> 4. Windows takes 60+ seconds to load drivers → programmer watchdog fires (8s) → crash → back to ZTE dump
> **The "8-second window" is a myth.** We were always talking to a dead PBL handle, never the actual programmer.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Prerequisites​
>
> #### Hardware​
>
> - REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
> - USB-C cable (data capable)
> - Windows PC (Linux/Mac can adapt)
>
> #### Software​
> powershell
>
> # Python 3.8+ with:
>
> pip install pyusb libusb
>
>
>
> # bkerler-edl (optional but helpful)
>
> git clone https://github.com/bkerler/edl
>
> cd edl
>
> pip install -r requirements.txt
>
>
>
> # Stock files (backup BEFORE modifying):
>
> - abl_b_dump.bin (from working device or extracted)
>
> - devprg.melf (extracted from ZTE dump mode)
>
>
> #### Files You'll Need​
>
>
>
>
>
> FileSourceSizedevprg.melfExtracted via EDL/ZTE dump~1.6MBabl_b_dump.binBackup of stock abl_b1MBinit_boot_b.imgStock from device/firmware8MBvbmeta_b.imgStock from device/firmware64KB
>

> ### Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode​
>
> #### The ONLY Reliable Method​
> powershell
>
> # 1. Unplug USB cable
>
> # 2. Press and hold BOTH Volume Up + Volume Down
>
> # 3. While holding buttons, plug USB cable back in
>
> # 4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds
>
> # 5. Device should appear as "Qualcomm HS-USB QDLoader 9008"
>
>
> #### Verify Connection​
> powershell
>
> Get-PnpDevice | Where-Object { $_.InstanceId -match "VID_05C6.*PID_9008" }
>
> # Should show: Status OK, FriendlyName contains "9008"
>
>
> #### Why This Works​
> This bypasses ZTE's crash handler entirely, putting the device in **PBL Sahara mode** with a clean USB state. The programmer will stay alive for ~8 seconds after loading.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 2: Backup Partitions​
>
> #### Get Partition Layout​
> From our working GPT dump, REDMAGIC 10 Pro LUN4 layout:
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Parse GPT (sector size 4096 bytes)
>
> vbmeta_b        start=490260  sectors=16    size=65,536 bytes
>
> init_boot_b     start=686048  sectors=2048  size=8,388,608 bytes
>
> abl_b           start=448832  sectors=256   size=1,048,576 bytes
>
> boot_b          start=683040  sectors=32768 size=134,217,728 bytes
>
>
> #### Dump Critical Partitions​
> Use this Python script while in 9008 mode:
>
>
>
> python
>
> # dump_partitions.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util, struct, time
>
>
>
> def find_9008():
>
>     dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>     if not dev:
>
>         print("No 9008 device found")
>
>         return None
>
>     return dev
>
>
>
> def sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions):
>
>     """Upload programmer and dump partitions via firehose"""
>
>     # ... (see Complete Scripts section)
>
>
>
> partitions = [
>
>     ("vbmeta_b", 490260, 16, "vbmeta_b_stock.img"),
>
>     ("init_boot_b", 686048, 2048, "init_boot_b_stock.img"),
>
>     ("abl_b", 448832, 256, "abl_b_stock.img"),
>
> ]
>
>
>
> dev = find_9008()
>
> if dev:
>
>     sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions)
>
>
