> ### Phase 3: Patch vbmeta​
>
> #### Why This is Critical​
> Flashing a modified init_boot_b without disabling vbmeta verification will trigger AVB failure:
>
>
>
>
> - **"Your device is corrupt"** screen
> - Boot loop back to ZTE dump
> - Rollback index mismatches
>
> #### Manual vbmeta Patch​
> python
>
> def patch_vbmeta_flags(input_file, output_file):
>
>     """Set AVB flags to 0x02 (verification disabled)"""
>
>     with open(input_file, 'rb') as f:
>
>         data = bytearray(f.read())
>
>
>
>     # Flags are at offset 12 (0x0C), 4-byte little-endian
>
>     # Change from 00 00 00 00 to 02 00 00 00
>
>     data[12:16] = b'\x02\x00\x00\x00'
>
>
>
>     with open(output_file, 'wb') as f:
>
>         f.write(data)
>
>     print(f"Patched {input_file} -> {output_file}")
>
>
>
> patch_vbmeta_flags("vbmeta_b_stock.img", "vbmeta_b_patched.img")
>
>
> #### Verify Patch​
> bash
>
> # Using avbtool (if available)
>
> avbtool info_image --image vbmeta_b_patched.img | grep "Flags"
>
> # Should show: Flags: 2
>
>
>
> # Or hexdump
>
> hexdump -C -n 64 vbmeta_b_patched.img | head
>
> # At offset 0x0C: 02 00 00 00
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 4: Root with Magisk​
>
> #### Step 1: Patch init_boot with Magisk​
> bash
>
> # On phone (after booting)
>
> # 1. Install Magisk APK
>
> # 2. Copy stock init_boot_b.img to /sdcard/Download/
>
> # 3. In Magisk app: Install → Select and Patch a File
>
> # 4. Choose init_boot_b.img
>
> # 5. Pull patched file: /sdcard/Download/magisk_patched.img
>
>
> #### Step 2: Prepare Files for EDL Flash​
> powershell
>
> # Files needed in working directory:
>
> - devprg.melf          # Programmer
>
> - vbmeta_b_patched.img # Patched vbmeta (64KB)
>
> - magisk_patched.img   # Patched init_boot (8MB)
>
>
> #### Step 3: Flash Both Partitions​
> Use the complete script below. **Critical**: Must flash in ONE EDL session with proper ZLP handling.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Complete Working Scripts​
>
> #### Script 1: Wait for Clean 9008​
> python
>
> # wait_9008.py
>
> import usb.core, time
>
>
>
> def wait_for_clean_9008(timeout=120):
>
>     """
>
>     Wait for device to enter clean 9008 mode via volume buttons.
>
>     Returns USB device object or None.
>
>     """
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print("CLEAN 9008 ENTRY INSTRUCTIONS:")
>
>     print("1. UNPLUG USB cable")
>
>     print("2. Press and hold BOTH VOLUME UP + VOLUME DOWN")
>
>     print("3. While holding, PLUG USB CABLE BACK IN")
>
>     print("4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds")
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print(f"\nWaiting up to {timeout} seconds for 9008 device...")
>
>
>
>     start = time.time()
>
>     while time.time() - start < timeout:
>
>         dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>         if dev:
>
>             print(f"\n![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) 9008 FOUND! bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")
>
>             return dev
>
>         if int(time.time() - start) % 10 == 0:
>
>             print(f"  {int(time.time() - start)}s...")
>
>         time.sleep(1)
>
>
>
>     print("\n![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found within timeout")
>
>     return None
>
>
>
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>
>     dev = wait_for_clean_9008()
>
>
> #### Script 2: Complete Flash (The One That Works)​
> python
>
> # root_redmagic.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util
>
> import struct, time, os
>
>
>
> # ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
>
> LUN = 4
>
> VBMETA_SECTOR = 490260
>
> VBMETA_SECTORS = 16
>
> INITBOOT_SECTOR = 686048
>
> INITBOOT_SECTORS = 2048  # 8MB
>
>
>
> PROG_FILE = "devprg.melf"
>
> VBMETA_PATCHED = "vbmeta_b_patched.img"
>
> INITBOOT_PATCHED = "magisk_patched.img"
>
>
>
> # ========== USB SETUP ==========
>
> def setup_usb(dev):
>
>     """Configure USB endpoints for Sahara/firehose"""
>
>     try:
>
>         if dev.is_kernel_driver_active(0):
>
>             dev.detach_kernel_driver(0)
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     try:
>
>         dev.set_configuration()
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     cfg = dev.get_active_configuration()
>
>     intf = cfg[(0,0)]
>
>
>
>     ep_out = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_OUT
>
>     )
>
>     ep_in = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_IN
>
>     )
>
>
>
>     return ep_out, ep_in
>
>
>
> def read_ep(ep, timeout=2000, size=4096):
>
>     """Safely read from endpoint"""
>
>     try:
>
>         return bytes(ep.read(size, timeout=timeout))
>
>     except:
>
>         return b''
>
>
>
> def write_ep(ep, data, timeout=5000):
>
>     """Safely write to endpoint"""
>
>     if isinstance(data, str):
>
>         data = data.encode()
>
>     try:
>
>         ep.write(data, timeout=timeout)
>
>         return True
>
>     except Exception as e:
>
>         print(f"  WRITE ERROR: {e}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
> # ========== SAHARA PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):
>
>     """
>
>     Upload programmer via Sahara.
>
>     Returns True if successful (38 chunks, DONE_RSP received)
>
>     """
>
>     print("\n=== SAHARA UPLOAD ===")
>
>
>
>     # Read HELLO
>
>     hello = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000, size=256)
>
>     if not hello or len(hello) < 24:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No Sahara HELLO received")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     cmd = struct.unpack('<I', hello[0:4])[0]
>
>     if cmd != 0x01:
>
>         print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Not HELLO: cmd=0x{cmd:x}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     ver = struct.unpack('<I', hello[8:12])[0]
>
>     verc = struct.unpack('<I', hello[12:16])[0]
>
>     mode = struct.unpack('<I', hello[20:24])[0]
>
>     print(f"HELLO: v{ver}/{verc} mode={mode}")
>
>
>
>     # Send HELLO_RESP (ALL ZEROS - CRITICAL!)
>
>     resp = struct.pack('<IIIIIIIIIIII',
>
>                        0x02, 0x30, ver, verc,
>
>                        0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, resp):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Upload loop
>
>     chunks = 0
>
>     while True:
>
>         pkt = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>         if not pkt:
>
>             print("![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Timeout waiting for command")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         cmd = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[0:4])[0]
>
>
>
>         if cmd == 0x12:  # READ_DATA_64
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[16:24])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[24:32])[0]
>
>             if chunks == 0:
>
>                 print(f"First READ_DATA_64: off={off} len={ln}")
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x03:  # READ_DATA
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[16:20])[0]
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x04:  # END_TRANSFER
>
>             status = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             print(f"END_TRANSFER: status={status} chunks={chunks}")
>
>
>
>             # Send DONE_REQ
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, struct.pack('<II', 0x05, 0x08))
>
>
>
>             # Read DONE_RSP
>
>             done = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>             if done:
>
>                 done_cmd = struct.unpack('<I', done[0:4])[0]
>
>                 print(f"DONE_RSP: cmd=0x{done_cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         else:
>
>             print(f"![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Unknown command: 0x{cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>     success = (chunks == 38)  # Known good count for devprg.melf
>
>     print(f"Sahara {'![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) SUCCESS' if success else '![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) FAILED'} ({chunks} chunks)")
>
>     return success

> # ========== FIREHOSE PROTOCOL ==========

> def firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):
>
>     """Send configure XML and wait for ACK"""

>     for i in range(20):

>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')

>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:

> ### Troubleshooting​
>
> #### "No 9008 device found"​
> **Problem:** Volume button method didn't work
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Try these alternatives:
>
> 1. Let battery die completely, then try volume buttons
>
> 2. From fastboot: fastboot reboot edl
>
> 3. From ADB (if bootable): adb reboot edl
>
> 4. Use EDL test point (last resort - requires opening phone)
>
>
> #### Sahara upload fails (not 38 chunks)​
> **Problem:** Wrong programmer or corrupted file
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Verify devprg.melf is correct
>
> python -c "
>
> data = open('devprg.melf','rb').read()
>
> print('Size:', len(data))
>
> print('ELF magic:', data[:4])
>
> print('Has firehose strings:', b'configure' in data)
>
> "
>
> # Should show: Size ~1.6MB, b'configure' found
>
>
> #### Configure NAK / No response​
> **Problem:** Programmer not starting firehose mode
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Ensure you entered **clean 9008** (volume buttons), NOT ZTE→9008
> - Try waiting 3 seconds after Sahara instead of 2
> - Check if USB reset happened (device should briefly disappear)
>
> #### Flash succeeds but phone won't boot​
> **Problem:** AVB still active or wrong partition
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Verify vbmeta patch
>
> with open('vbmeta_b_patched.img','rb') as f:
>
>     data = f.read()
>
> print(f"Flags at offset 12: {data[12:16].hex()}")
>
> # Should show: 02000000
>
>
> #### Phone stuck at "Your device is corrupt"​
> **Problem:** vbmeta verification still enabled
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Re-flash with proper vbmeta patch (flags=2)
> - Check if you flashed to correct slot (make sure it's _b)
> - Consider flashing both slots if unsure
>
> #### Windows can't find device after Sahara​
> **Problem:** USB re-enumeration timing
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Use the script above - it reconnects properly
> - Don't use Zadig or change drivers - libusb backend works
> - If using Zadig, install WinUSB for 9008 mode
>
>
>
> ### FAQ​
>
> #### Q: Is devprg.melf the correct programmer?​
> **A:** Yes! It contains firehose protocol strings (configure, rawmode, program, UFS). The issue was never the programmer - it was USB re-enumeration.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Why doesn't ZTE → SWITCH_MODE work?​
> **A:** The ZTE crash handler leaves USB in a dirty state. After transition, the programmer's USB reset creates a new device that Windows takes 60+ seconds to enumerate - by then the programmer has crashed (8s watchdog).
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What's with the Zero Length Packet (ZLP)?​
> **A:** Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" expects a ZLP after data transfers that are exact multiples of USB packet size. 8MB (8388608 bytes) is a multiple of 512/1024, so a ZLP is required. Sending ZLP after every chunk corrupts the data.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Do I need to flash both slots?​
> **A:** For safety, flash only slot B if that's your active slot. Check with:
>
>
>
> bash
>
> # In fastboot
>
> fastboot getvar current-slot
>
> If unsure, you can flash both - just adjust sector addresses from GPT.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What about other vbmeta partitions (system, vendor)?​
> **A:** The main vbmeta controls boot image verification. If you're only modifying init_boot, patching main vbmeta is sufficient. If you modify system/vendor later, you'll need to patch those too.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Will this work on other REDMAGIC models?​
> **A:** The principles apply, but partition addresses will differ. You'll need to dump GPT from your specific model first.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: My phone won't enter 9008 at all!​
> **A:** Last resort - EDL test point. Requires opening the phone and shorting specific pads. Check XDA for your model's test point location.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Is the bootloader unlocked after this?​
> **A:** No - this method bypasses the bootloader entirely via EDL. The bootloader remains locked. You're rooted with a locked bootloader, which is possible on Qualcomm devices via EDL.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Partition Reference (REDMAGIC 10 Pro - NX789J)​
>
> #### LUN4 GPT (User Data/System Partitions)​
> text
>
> Partition           Start Sector    Sectors     Size
>
> ------------------  -------------   --------    --------
>
> xbl_b               184             15360       60MB
>
> abl_b               448832          256         1MB
>
> boot_b              683040          32768       128MB
>
> init_boot_b         686048          2048        8MB
>
> vbmeta_b            490260          16          64KB
>
> vbmeta_system_b     520120          16          64KB
>
> vbmeta_vendor_b     492584          16          64KB
>
>
> #### Critical Addresses for Rooting​
> python
>
> VBMETA_B = {
>
>     'lun': 4,
>
>     'start': 490260,
>
>     'sectors': 16,
>
>     'size': 65536
>
> }
>
>
>
> INIT_BOOT_B = {
>
>     'lun': 4,
>
>     'start': 686048,
>
>     'sectors': 2048,
>
>     'size': 8388608
>
> }
>
>
>
> **The most important lesson:** Don't trust the 8-second window. The programmer is alive for ~8 seconds, but you have to catch it in the first 2 seconds after USB re-enumeration. The volume button method gives you a clean state where the programmer stays alive and the USB handle remains valid.
>
>
>
> **The ZLP (Zero Length Packet) issue** cost us 10+ hours. Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" is strict about protocol - one ZLP at the end, not after every chunk.
>
>
>
> **vbmeta is NOT optional** - if you flash a modified init_boot without patching vbmeta, you'll get "device is corrupt" every time. Patch flags to 0x02.
>
>
>
> **The programmer IS correct** - devprg.melf from ZTE dump mode is a valid firehose programmer. Don't waste time searching for another one.
>
>
>
>
>
> *This guide represents 26+ hours of debugging across 50+ scripts, 3 USB protocol analyzers, and 2 near-brick scares. I will share freely on XDA and help others avoid the same pitfalls.*

### #430 — **rootNv** · Feb 23, 2026 at 9:55 AM · page 22

> **BD_Security said:**
> ### REDMAGIC 10 Pro - Complete EDL Recovery & Root Guide​
> *Based on 26+ hours of debugging a bricked device*
>
>
>
>
> ### Table of Contents​
>
> 1. The Problem
> 2. Critical Discoveries
> 3. Prerequisites
> 4. Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode
> 5. Phase 2: Backup Partitions
> 6. Phase 3: Patch vbmeta
> 7. Phase 4: Root with Magisk
> 8. Complete Working Scripts
> 9. Troubleshooting
> 10. FAQ
>
>
>
> ### The Problem​
>
> - Device stuck in **ZTE MemoryDump Mode** (VID_19D2![:p](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ID_0112)
> - Phone displays: *"Your device is corrupt and will not boot"*
> - Custom scripts fail with USB errors or programmer crashes
> - Sahara upload works (38 chunks) but firehose never starts
>
> ### Critical Discoveries​
>
> #### What DOESN'T Work ​
>
> - **ZTE → SWITCH_MODE → 9008 transition** (corrupts USB state, kills programmer)
> - clear_halt() after Sahara DONE (hangs 6-8 seconds, misses programmer window)
> - Reconnecting to same handle after programmer starts (device disappears)
> - Zero Length Packet (ZLP) after every chunk (corrupts data)
> - Using 1,2,3,4,5,6 in HELLO_RESP reserved bytes (causes mode mismatch)
>
> #### What DOES Work ​
>
> 1. **Clean 9008 entry** via volume buttons (bypass ZTE crash handler)
> 2. **Exact Sahara protocol** from edl_v5 (all-zero reserved bytes)
> 3. **NO post-DONE delays** - read immediately
> 4. **Continuous data + ONE ZLP** at the very end
> 5. **Flash BOTH** patched init_boot AND patched vbmeta
> 6. **Direct 9008 entry** = success. **ZTE transition** = failure.
>
> #### The Real Insight ​
> The programmer (devprg.melf) **IS** valid - it contains both XBL boot code AND firehose protocol strings (rawmode, configure, program, UFS). Sahara uploads 38 chunks successfully every time with DONE_RSP status=0.
>
>
>
> The problem: After Sahara DONE, the programmer:
>
>
>
>
> 1. Restarts the USB controller
> 2. Re-enumerates as a NEW 9008 device (pkt=512 → pkt=1024)
> 3. Our old USB handle dies → Errno 19: No such device
> 4. Windows takes 60+ seconds to load drivers → programmer watchdog fires (8s) → crash → back to ZTE dump
> **The "8-second window" is a myth.** We were always talking to a dead PBL handle, never the actual programmer.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Prerequisites​
>
> #### Hardware​
>
> - REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
> - USB-C cable (data capable)
> - Windows PC (Linux/Mac can adapt)
>
> #### Software​
> powershell
>
> # Python 3.8+ with:
>
> pip install pyusb libusb
>
>
>
> # bkerler-edl (optional but helpful)
>
> git clone https://github.com/bkerler/edl
>
> cd edl
>
> pip install -r requirements.txt
>
>
>
> # Stock files (backup BEFORE modifying):
>
> - abl_b_dump.bin (from working device or extracted)
>
> - devprg.melf (extracted from ZTE dump mode)
>
>
> #### Files You'll Need​
>
>
>
>
>
> FileSourceSizedevprg.melfExtracted via EDL/ZTE dump~1.6MBabl_b_dump.binBackup of stock abl_b1MBinit_boot_b.imgStock from device/firmware8MBvbmeta_b.imgStock from device/firmware64KB
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode​
>
> #### The ONLY Reliable Method​
> powershell
>
> # 1. Unplug USB cable
>
> # 2. Press and hold BOTH Volume Up + Volume Down
>
> # 3. While holding buttons, plug USB cable back in
>
> # 4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds
>
> # 5. Device should appear as "Qualcomm HS-USB QDLoader 9008"
>
>
> #### Verify Connection​
> powershell
>
> Get-PnpDevice | Where-Object { $_.InstanceId -match "VID_05C6.*PID_9008" }
>
> # Should show: Status OK, FriendlyName contains "9008"
>
>
> #### Why This Works​
> This bypasses ZTE's crash handler entirely, putting the device in **PBL Sahara mode** with a clean USB state. The programmer will stay alive for ~8 seconds after loading.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 2: Backup Partitions​
>
> #### Get Partition Layout​
> From our working GPT dump, REDMAGIC 10 Pro LUN4 layout:
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Parse GPT (sector size 4096 bytes)
>
> vbmeta_b        start=490260  sectors=16    size=65,536 bytes
>
> init_boot_b     start=686048  sectors=2048  size=8,388,608 bytes
>
> abl_b           start=448832  sectors=256   size=1,048,576 bytes
>
> boot_b          start=683040  sectors=32768 size=134,217,728 bytes
>
>
> #### Dump Critical Partitions​
> Use this Python script while in 9008 mode:
>
>
>
> python
>
> # dump_partitions.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util, struct, time
>
>
>
> def find_9008():
>
>     dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>     if not dev:
>
>         print("No 9008 device found")
>
>         return None
>
>     return dev
>
>
>
> def sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions):
>
>     """Upload programmer and dump partitions via firehose"""
>
>     # ... (see Complete Scripts section)
>
>
>
> partitions = [
>
>     ("vbmeta_b", 490260, 16, "vbmeta_b_stock.img"),
>
>     ("init_boot_b", 686048, 2048, "init_boot_b_stock.img"),
>
>     ("abl_b", 448832, 256, "abl_b_stock.img"),
>
> ]
>
>
>
> dev = find_9008()
>
> if dev:
>
>     sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions)
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 3: Patch vbmeta​
>
> #### Why This is Critical​
> Flashing a modified init_boot_b without disabling vbmeta verification will trigger AVB failure:
>
>
>
>
> - **"Your device is corrupt"** screen
> - Boot loop back to ZTE dump
> - Rollback index mismatches
>
> #### Manual vbmeta Patch​
> python
>
> def patch_vbmeta_flags(input_file, output_file):
>
>     """Set AVB flags to 0x02 (verification disabled)"""
>
>     with open(input_file, 'rb') as f:
>
>         data = bytearray(f.read())
>
>
>
>     # Flags are at offset 12 (0x0C), 4-byte little-endian
>
>     # Change from 00 00 00 00 to 02 00 00 00
>
>     data[12:16] = b'\x02\x00\x00\x00'
>
>
>
>     with open(output_file, 'wb') as f:
>
>         f.write(data)
>
>     print(f"Patched {input_file} -> {output_file}")
>
>
>
> patch_vbmeta_flags("vbmeta_b_stock.img", "vbmeta_b_patched.img")
>
>
> #### Verify Patch​
> bash
>
> # Using avbtool (if available)
>
> avbtool info_image --image vbmeta_b_patched.img | grep "Flags"
>
> # Should show: Flags: 2
>
>
>
> # Or hexdump
>
> hexdump -C -n 64 vbmeta_b_patched.img | head
>
> # At offset 0x0C: 02 00 00 00
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 4: Root with Magisk​
>
> #### Step 1: Patch init_boot with Magisk​
> bash
>
> # On phone (after booting)
>
> # 1. Install Magisk APK
>
> # 2. Copy stock init_boot_b.img to /sdcard/Download/
>
> # 3. In Magisk app: Install → Select and Patch a File
>
> # 4. Choose init_boot_b.img
>
> # 5. Pull patched file: /sdcard/Download/magisk_patched.img
>
>
> #### Step 2: Prepare Files for EDL Flash​
> powershell
>
> # Files needed in working directory:
>
> - devprg.melf          # Programmer
>
> - vbmeta_b_patched.img # Patched vbmeta (64KB)
>
> - magisk_patched.img   # Patched init_boot (8MB)
>
>
> #### Step 3: Flash Both Partitions​
> Use the complete script below. **Critical**: Must flash in ONE EDL session with proper ZLP handling.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Complete Working Scripts​
>
> #### Script 1: Wait for Clean 9008​
> python
>
> # wait_9008.py
>
> import usb.core, time
>
>
>
> def wait_for_clean_9008(timeout=120):
>
>     """
>
>     Wait for device to enter clean 9008 mode via volume buttons.
>
>     Returns USB device object or None.
>
>     """
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print("CLEAN 9008 ENTRY INSTRUCTIONS:")
>
>     print("1. UNPLUG USB cable")
>
>     print("2. Press and hold BOTH VOLUME UP + VOLUME DOWN")
>
>     print("3. While holding, PLUG USB CABLE BACK IN")
>
>     print("4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds")
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print(f"\nWaiting up to {timeout} seconds for 9008 device...")
>
>
>
>     start = time.time()
>
>     while time.time() - start < timeout:
>
>         dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>         if dev:
>
>             print(f"\n![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) 9008 FOUND! bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")
>
>             return dev
>
>         if int(time.time() - start) % 10 == 0:
>
>             print(f"  {int(time.time() - start)}s...")
>
>         time.sleep(1)
>
>
>
>     print("\n![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found within timeout")
>
>     return None
>
>
>
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>
>     dev = wait_for_clean_9008()
>
>
> #### Script 2: Complete Flash (The One That Works)​
> python
>
> # root_redmagic.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util
>
> import struct, time, os
>
>
>
> # ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
>
> LUN = 4
>
> VBMETA_SECTOR = 490260
>
> VBMETA_SECTORS = 16
>
> INITBOOT_SECTOR = 686048
>
> INITBOOT_SECTORS = 2048  # 8MB
>
>
>
> PROG_FILE = "devprg.melf"
>
> VBMETA_PATCHED = "vbmeta_b_patched.img"
>
> INITBOOT_PATCHED = "magisk_patched.img"
>
>
>
> # ========== USB SETUP ==========
>
> def setup_usb(dev):
>
>     """Configure USB endpoints for Sahara/firehose"""
>
>     try:
>
>         if dev.is_kernel_driver_active(0):
>
>             dev.detach_kernel_driver(0)
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     try:
>
>         dev.set_configuration()
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     cfg = dev.get_active_configuration()
>
>     intf = cfg[(0,0)]
>
>
>
>     ep_out = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_OUT
>
>     )
>
>     ep_in = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_IN
>
>     )
>
>
>
>     return ep_out, ep_in
>
>
>
> def read_ep(ep, timeout=2000, size=4096):
>
>     """Safely read from endpoint"""
>
>     try:
>
>         return bytes(ep.read(size, timeout=timeout))
>
>     except:
>
>         return b''
>
>
>
> def write_ep(ep, data, timeout=5000):
>
>     """Safely write to endpoint"""
>
>     if isinstance(data, str):
>
>         data = data.encode()
>
>     try:
>
>         ep.write(data, timeout=timeout)
>
>         return True
>
>     except Exception as e:
>
>         print(f"  WRITE ERROR: {e}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
> # ========== SAHARA PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):
>
>     """
>
>     Upload programmer via Sahara.
>
>     Returns True if successful (38 chunks, DONE_RSP received)
>
>     """
>
>     print("\n=== SAHARA UPLOAD ===")
>
>
>
>     # Read HELLO
>
>     hello = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000, size=256)
>
>     if not hello or len(hello) < 24:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No Sahara HELLO received")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     cmd = struct.unpack('<I', hello[0:4])[0]
>
>     if cmd != 0x01:
>
>         print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Not HELLO: cmd=0x{cmd:x}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     ver = struct.unpack('<I', hello[8:12])[0]
>
>     verc = struct.unpack('<I', hello[12:16])[0]
>
>     mode = struct.unpack('<I', hello[20:24])[0]
>
>     print(f"HELLO: v{ver}/{verc} mode={mode}")
>
>
>
>     # Send HELLO_RESP (ALL ZEROS - CRITICAL!)
>
>     resp = struct.pack('<IIIIIIIIIIII',
>
>                        0x02, 0x30, ver, verc,
>
>                        0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, resp):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Upload loop
>
>     chunks = 0
>
>     while True:
>
>         pkt = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>         if not pkt:
>
>             print("![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Timeout waiting for command")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         cmd = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[0:4])[0]
>
>
>
>         if cmd == 0x12:  # READ_DATA_64
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[16:24])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[24:32])[0]
>
>             if chunks == 0:
>
>                 print(f"First READ_DATA_64: off={off} len={ln}")
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x03:  # READ_DATA
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[16:20])[0]
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x04:  # END_TRANSFER
>
>             status = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             print(f"END_TRANSFER: status={status} chunks={chunks}")
>
>
>
>             # Send DONE_REQ
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, struct.pack('<II', 0x05, 0x08))
>
>
>
>             # Read DONE_RSP
>
>             done = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>             if done:
>
>                 done_cmd = struct.unpack('<I', done[0:4])[0]
>
>                 print(f"DONE_RSP: cmd=0x{done_cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         else:
>
>             print(f"![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Unknown command: 0x{cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>     success = (chunks == 38)  # Known good count for devprg.melf
>
>     print(f"Sahara {'![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) SUCCESS' if success else '![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) FAILED'} ({chunks} chunks)")
>
>     return success
>
>
>
> # ========== FIREHOSE PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):
>
>     """Send configure XML and wait for ACK"""
>
>     print("\n=== CONFIGURING FIREHOSE ===")
>
>
>
>     cfg_xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?><data><configure MemoryName="UFS" Verbose="0" AlwaysValidate="0" MaxDigestTableSizeInBytes="2048" MaxPayloadSizeToTargetInBytes="1048576" ZLPAwareHost="1" SkipStorageInit="0" SkipWrite="0" Oem="ZTE"/></data>'
>
>
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, cfg_xml):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Wait for ACK (up to 10s)
>
>     for i in range(20):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=1000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Configure ACK received")
>
>                 return True
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Configure NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.5)
>
>
>
>     print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No configure response")
>
>     return False
>
>
>
> def firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, data, start_sector, num_sectors, name):
>
>     """
>
>     Flash data to partition.
>
>     CRITICAL: Send ALL data, then ONE ZLP at the end
>
>     """
>
>     print(f"\n=== PROGRAMMING {name} ===")
>
>     print(f"Start sector: {start_sector}, Sectors: {num_sectors}, Size: {len(data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     # Send program command
>
>     prog_xml = f'<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><program SECTOR_SIZE_IN_BYTES="4096" num_partition_sectors="{num_sectors}" physical_partition_number="{LUN}" start_sector="{start_sector}" filename="{name}"/></data>'
>
>
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, prog_xml):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Wait for rawmode ACK
>
>     rawmode = False
>
>     for i in range(30):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'rawmode="true"' in txt.lower() and 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 rawmode = True
>
>                 break
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Program NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.2)
>
>
>
>     if not rawmode:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No rawmode ACK")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Rawmode ACK received, sending data...")
>
>
>
>     # Send ALL data continuously
>
>     sent = 0
>
>     chunk_size = 65536  # 64KB chunks for USB
>
>     while sent < len(data):
>
>         end = min(sent + chunk_size, len(data))
>
>         if not write_ep(ep_out, data[sent:end], timeout=30000):
>
>             print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Write failed at {sent}/{len(data)}")
>
>             return False
>
>         sent = end
>
>         if sent % 262144 == 0 or sent == len(data):
>
>             print(f"  Sent {sent}/{len(data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     # CRITICAL: Send Zero Length Packet at the very end
>
>     print("Sending ZLP...")
>
>     write_ep(ep_out, b"", timeout=1000)
>
>
>
>     # Wait for final ACK
>
>     print("Waiting for flash ACK...")
>
>     for i in range(60):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:200]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) {name} flashed successfully!")
>
>                 return True
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) {name} flash NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.5)
>
>
>
>     print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No final ACK for {name}")
>
>     return False
>
>
>
> # ========== MAIN ==========
>
> def main():
>
>     print("=" * 70)
>
>     print("REDMAGIC 10 Pro - EDL Root Script")
>
>     print("=" * 70)
>
>
>
>     # Wait for clean 9008
>
>     print("\n[1/5] Waiting for clean 9008 mode...")
>
>     print("Follow instructions above, then press Enter when ready")
>
>     input()
>
>
>
>     dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>     if not dev:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Found 9008: bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")
>
>
>
>     # Setup USB
>
>     print("\n[2/5] Setting up USB...")
>
>     ep_out, ep_in = setup_usb(dev)
>
>     print(f"Endpoints: OUT=0x{ep_out.bEndpointAddress:x} IN=0x{ep_in.bEndpointAddress:x}")
>
>     print(f"Max packet: {ep_in.wMaxPacketSize}")
>
>
>
>     # Load programmer
>
>     print("\n[3/5] Loading programmer...")
>
>     with open(PROG_FILE, 'rb') as f:
>
>         prog_data = f.read()
>
>     print(f"Programmer size: {len(prog_data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     if not sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Sahara upload failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Wait for programmer to start
>
>     print("\nWaiting 2 seconds for programmer to initialize...")
>
>     time.sleep(2)
>
>
>
>     # Configure firehose
>
>     if not firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Firehose configure failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Load patched vbmeta
>
>     print("\n[4/5] Loading patched vbmeta...")
>
>     with open(VBMETA_PATCHED, 'rb') as f:
>
>         vbmeta_data = f.read()
>
>     print(f"vbmeta_b size: {len(vbmeta_data)} bytes (should be 65536)")
>
>
>
>     # Flash vbmeta_b
>
>     if not firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, vbmeta_data, VBMETA_SECTOR, VBMETA_SECTORS, "vbmeta_b"):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) vbmeta_b flash failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Load patched init_boot
>
>     print("\n[5/5] Loading patched init_boot...")
>
>     with open(INITBOOT_PATCHED, 'rb') as f:
>
>         init_data = f.read()
>
>     print(f"init_boot_b size: {len(init_data)} bytes (should be 8388608)")
>
>
>
>     # Flash init_boot_b
>
>     if not firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, init_data, INITBOOT_SECTOR, INITBOOT_SECTORS, "init_boot_b"):
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) init_boot_b flash failed")
>
>         return
>
>
>
>     # Success!
>
>     print("\n" + "=" * 70)
>
>     print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) ROOT SUCCESSFUL! ![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png)")
>
>     print("=" * 70)
>
>     print("\nSending reboot command...")
>
>
>
>     # Reboot
>
>     write_ep(ep_out, '<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><power value="reset"/></data>')
>
>     time.sleep(1)
>
>
>
>     print("\nPhone should now boot with Magisk installed!")
>
>     print("First boot may take 2-3 minutes.")
>
>
>
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>
>     main()
>
>
>
>
> ### Troubleshooting​
>
> #### "No 9008 device found"​
> **Problem:** Volume button method didn't work
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Try these alternatives:
>
> 1. Let battery die completely, then try volume buttons
>
> 2. From fastboot: fastboot reboot edl
>
> 3. From ADB (if bootable): adb reboot edl
>
> 4. Use EDL test point (last resort - requires opening phone)
>
>
> #### Sahara upload fails (not 38 chunks)​
> **Problem:** Wrong programmer or corrupted file
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Verify devprg.melf is correct
>
> python -c "
>
> data = open('devprg.melf','rb').read()
>
> print('Size:', len(data))
>
> print('ELF magic:', data[:4])
>
> print('Has firehose strings:', b'configure' in data)
>
> "
>
> # Should show: Size ~1.6MB, b'configure' found
>
>
> #### Configure NAK / No response​
> **Problem:** Programmer not starting firehose mode
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Ensure you entered **clean 9008** (volume buttons), NOT ZTE→9008
> - Try waiting 3 seconds after Sahara instead of 2
> - Check if USB reset happened (device should briefly disappear)
>
> #### Flash succeeds but phone won't boot​
> **Problem:** AVB still active or wrong partition
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Verify vbmeta patch
>
> with open('vbmeta_b_patched.img','rb') as f:
>
>     data = f.read()
>
> print(f"Flags at offset 12: {data[12:16].hex()}")
>
> # Should show: 02000000
>
>
> #### Phone stuck at "Your device is corrupt"​
> **Problem:** vbmeta verification still enabled
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Re-flash with proper vbmeta patch (flags=2)
> - Check if you flashed to correct slot (make sure it's _b)
> - Consider flashing both slots if unsure
>
> #### Windows can't find device after Sahara​
> **Problem:** USB re-enumeration timing
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Use the script above - it reconnects properly
> - Don't use Zadig or change drivers - libusb backend works
> - If using Zadig, install WinUSB for 9008 mode
>
>
>
> ### FAQ​
>
> #### Q: Is devprg.melf the correct programmer?​
> **A:** Yes! It contains firehose protocol strings (configure, rawmode, program, UFS). The issue was never the programmer - it was USB re-enumeration.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Why doesn't ZTE → SWITCH_MODE work?​
> **A:** The ZTE crash handler leaves USB in a dirty state. After transition, the programmer's USB reset creates a new device that Windows takes 60+ seconds to enumerate - by then the programmer has crashed (8s watchdog).
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What's with the Zero Length Packet (ZLP)?​
> **A:** Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" expects a ZLP after data transfers that are exact multiples of USB packet size. 8MB (8388608 bytes) is a multiple of 512/1024, so a ZLP is required. Sending ZLP after every chunk corrupts the data.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Do I need to flash both slots?​
> **A:** For safety, flash only slot B if that's your active slot. Check with:
>
>
>
> bash
>
> # In fastboot
>
> fastboot getvar current-slot
>
> If unsure, you can flash both - just adjust sector addresses from GPT.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What about other vbmeta partitions (system, vendor)?​
> **A:** The main vbmeta controls boot image verification. If you're only modifying init_boot, patching main vbmeta is sufficient. If you modify system/vendor later, you'll need to patch those too.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Will this work on other REDMAGIC models?​
> **A:** The principles apply, but partition addresses will differ. You'll need to dump GPT from your specific model first.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: My phone won't enter 9008 at all!​
> **A:** Last resort - EDL test point. Requires opening the phone and shorting specific pads. Check XDA for your model's test point location.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Is the bootloader unlocked after this?​
> **A:** No - this method bypasses the bootloader entirely via EDL. The bootloader remains locked. You're rooted with a locked bootloader, which is possible on Qualcomm devices via EDL.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Partition Reference (REDMAGIC 10 Pro - NX789J)​
>
> #### LUN4 GPT (User Data/System Partitions)​
> text
>
> Разделение Начало Сектор Секторы Размер
>
> ------------------ ------------- -------- --------
>
> xbl_b 184 15360 60 МБ
>
> abl_b 448832 256 1MB
>
> boot_b 683040 32768 128MB
>
> init_boot_b 686048 2048 8MB
>
> vbmeta_b 490260 16 64KB
>
> vbmeta_system_b 520120 16 64KB
>
> vbmeta_vendor_b 492584 16 64KB
>
>
> #### Критические адреса для получения root-прав​
> питон
>
> VBMETA_B = {
>
>     'лун': 4,
>
>     'start': 490260,
>
>     'сектора': 16,
>
>     'размер': 65536
>
> }
>
>
>
> INIT_BOOT_B = {
>
>     'лун': 4,
>
>     'start': 686048,
>
>     'секторов': 2048,
>
>     'размер': 8388608
>
> }
>
>
>
> **Самый важный урок:** не доверяйте 8-секундному окну. Программатор работает примерно 8 секунд, но вы должны застать его в первые 2 секунды после повторного перечисления USB. Метод с кнопкой регулировки громкости обеспечивает чистое состояние, при котором программатор остается активным, а дескриптор USB — действительным.
>
>
>
> **Проблема с пакетами нулевой длины (ZLP)** отняла у нас более 10 часов. Firehose с параметром ZLPAwareHost="1" строго соблюдает протокол — один пакет ZLP в конце, а не после каждого фрагмента.
>
>
>
> **Параметр vbmeta НЕ является необязательным** — если вы прошьете модифицированный init_boot без патча vbmeta, вы будете получать сообщение «устройство повреждено» каждый раз. Установите флаги патча на 0x02.
>
>
>
> **Программист прав** — devprg.melf из режима дампа ZTE является допустимым программатором Firehose. Не тратьте время на поиски другого.
>
>
>
>
>
> *Это руководство основано на более чем 26 часах отладки более 50 скриптов, 3 анализаторах USB-протоколов и 2 случаях, когда устройство чуть не вышло из строя. Я поделюсь результатами на XDA и помогу другим избежать подобных ошибок.*
>
>
>
> **Последнее обновление:** февраль 2025 г.
>
> **Устройство:** REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
>
> **Версия Android:** 15
>
> **Ядро:** совместимо с GKI

### #432 — **mark332** · Feb 23, 2026 at 5:43 PM · page 22

> **BD_Security said:**
> ### REDMAGIC 10 Pro - Complete EDL Recovery & Root Guide​
> *Based on 26+ hours of debugging a bricked device*
>
>
>
>
> ### Table of Contents​
>
> 1. The Problem
> 2. Critical Discoveries
> 3. Prerequisites
> 4. Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode
> 5. Phase 2: Backup Partitions
> 6. Phase 3: Patch vbmeta
> 7. Phase 4: Root with Magisk
> 8. Complete Working Scripts
> 9. Troubleshooting
> 10. FAQ
>
>
>
> ### The Problem​
>
> - Device stuck in **ZTE MemoryDump Mode** (VID_19D2![:p](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ID_0112)
> - Phone displays: *"Your device is corrupt and will not boot"*
> - Custom scripts fail with USB errors or programmer crashes
> - Sahara upload works (38 chunks) but firehose never starts
>
> ### Critical Discoveries​
>
> #### What DOESN'T Work ​
>
> - **ZTE → SWITCH_MODE → 9008 transition** (corrupts USB state, kills programmer)
> - clear_halt() after Sahara DONE (hangs 6-8 seconds, misses programmer window)
> - Reconnecting to same handle after programmer starts (device disappears)
> - Zero Length Packet (ZLP) after every chunk (corrupts data)
> - Using 1,2,3,4,5,6 in HELLO_RESP reserved bytes (causes mode mismatch)
>
> #### What DOES Work ​
>
> 1. **Clean 9008 entry** via volume buttons (bypass ZTE crash handler)
> 2. **Exact Sahara protocol** from edl_v5 (all-zero reserved bytes)
> 3. **NO post-DONE delays** - read immediately
> 4. **Continuous data + ONE ZLP** at the very end
> 5. **Flash BOTH** patched init_boot AND patched vbmeta
> 6. **Direct 9008 entry** = success. **ZTE transition** = failure.
>
> #### The Real Insight ​
> The programmer (devprg.melf) **IS** valid - it contains both XBL boot code AND firehose protocol strings (rawmode, configure, program, UFS). Sahara uploads 38 chunks successfully every time with DONE_RSP status=0.
>
>
>
> The problem: After Sahara DONE, the programmer:
>
>
>
>
> 1. Restarts the USB controller
> 2. Re-enumerates as a NEW 9008 device (pkt=512 → pkt=1024)
> 3. Our old USB handle dies → Errno 19: No such device
> 4. Windows takes 60+ seconds to load drivers → programmer watchdog fires (8s) → crash → back to ZTE dump
> **The "8-second window" is a myth.** We were always talking to a dead PBL handle, never the actual programmer.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Prerequisites​
>
> #### Hardware​
>
> - REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
> - USB-C cable (data capable)
> - Windows PC (Linux/Mac can adapt)
>
> #### Software​
> powershell
>
> # Python 3.8+ with:
>
> pip install pyusb libusb
>
>
>
> # bkerler-edl (optional but helpful)
>
> git clone https://github.com/bkerler/edl
>
> cd edl
>
> pip install -r requirements.txt
>
>
>
> # Stock files (backup BEFORE modifying):
>
> - abl_b_dump.bin (from working device or extracted)
>
> - devprg.melf (extracted from ZTE dump mode)
>
>
> #### Files You'll Need​
>
>
>
>
>
> FileSourceSizedevprg.melfExtracted via EDL/ZTE dump~1.6MBabl_b_dump.binBackup of stock abl_b1MBinit_boot_b.imgStock from device/firmware8MBvbmeta_b.imgStock from device/firmware64KB
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 1: Enter Clean 9008 Mode​
>
> #### The ONLY Reliable Method​
> powershell
>
> # 1. Unplug USB cable
>
> # 2. Press and hold BOTH Volume Up + Volume Down
>
> # 3. While holding buttons, plug USB cable back in
>
> # 4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds
>
> # 5. Device should appear as "Qualcomm HS-USB QDLoader 9008"
>
>
> #### Verify Connection​
> powershell
>
> Get-PnpDevice | Where-Object { $_.InstanceId -match "VID_05C6.*PID_9008" }
>
> # Should show: Status OK, FriendlyName contains "9008"
>
>
> #### Why This Works​
> This bypasses ZTE's crash handler entirely, putting the device in **PBL Sahara mode** with a clean USB state. The programmer will stay alive for ~8 seconds after loading.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 2: Backup Partitions​
>
> #### Get Partition Layout​
> From our working GPT dump, REDMAGIC 10 Pro LUN4 layout:
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Parse GPT (sector size 4096 bytes)
>
> vbmeta_b        start=490260  sectors=16    size=65,536 bytes
>
> init_boot_b     start=686048  sectors=2048  size=8,388,608 bytes
>
> abl_b           start=448832  sectors=256   size=1,048,576 bytes
>
> boot_b          start=683040  sectors=32768 size=134,217,728 bytes
>
>
> #### Dump Critical Partitions​
> Use this Python script while in 9008 mode:
>
>
>
> python
>
> # dump_partitions.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util, struct, time
>
>
>
> def find_9008():
>
>     dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>     if not dev:
>
>         print("No 9008 device found")
>
>         return None
>
>     return dev
>
>
>

>
>     """Upload programmer and dump partitions via firehose"""
>
>     # ... (see Complete Scripts section)
>
>

> partitions = [
>
>     ("vbmeta_b", 490260, 16, "vbmeta_b_stock.img"),
>
>     ("init_boot_b", 686048, 2048, "init_boot_b_stock.img"),
>
>     ("abl_b", 448832, 256, "abl_b_stock.img"),
>
> ]
>
>
>
> dev = find_9008()
>
> if dev:
>
>     sahara_upload_and_dump(dev, partitions)
>
>

> ### Phase 3: Patch vbmeta​
>
> #### Why This is Critical​
> Flashing a modified init_boot_b without disabling vbmeta verification will trigger AVB failure:
>
>
>
>
> - **"Your device is corrupt"** screen
> - Boot loop back to ZTE dump
> - Rollback index mismatches
>
> #### Manual vbmeta Patch​
> python
>
> def patch_vbmeta_flags(input_file, output_file):
>
>     """Set AVB flags to 0x02 (verification disabled)"""
>
>     with open(input_file, 'rb') as f:
>
>         data = bytearray(f.read())
>
>
>
>     # Flags are at offset 12 (0x0C), 4-byte little-endian
>
>     # Change from 00 00 00 00 to 02 00 00 00
>
>     data[12:16] = b'\x02\x00\x00\x00'
>
>
>
>     with open(output_file, 'wb') as f:
>
>         f.write(data)
>
>     print(f"Patched {input_file} -> {output_file}")
>
>
>
> patch_vbmeta_flags("vbmeta_b_stock.img", "vbmeta_b_patched.img")
>
>
> #### Verify Patch​
> bash
>
> # Using avbtool (if available)
>
> avbtool info_image --image vbmeta_b_patched.img | grep "Flags"
>
> # Should show: Flags: 2
>
>
>
> # Or hexdump
>
> hexdump -C -n 64 vbmeta_b_patched.img | head
>
> # At offset 0x0C: 02 00 00 00
>
>
>
>
> ### Phase 4: Root with Magisk​
>
> #### Step 1: Patch init_boot with Magisk​
> bash
>
> # On phone (after booting)
>
> # 1. Install Magisk APK
>
> # 2. Copy stock init_boot_b.img to /sdcard/Download/
>
> # 3. In Magisk app: Install → Select and Patch a File
>
> # 4. Choose init_boot_b.img
>
> # 5. Pull patched file: /sdcard/Download/magisk_patched.img
>
>
> #### Step 2: Prepare Files for EDL Flash​
> powershell
>
> # Files needed in working directory:
>
> - devprg.melf          # Programmer
>
> - vbmeta_b_patched.img # Patched vbmeta (64KB)
>
> - magisk_patched.img   # Patched init_boot (8MB)
>
>
> #### Step 3: Flash Both Partitions​
> Use the complete script below. **Critical**: Must flash in ONE EDL session with proper ZLP handling.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Complete Working Scripts​
>
> #### Script 1: Wait for Clean 9008​
> python
>
> # wait_9008.py
>
> import usb.core, time
>
>
>
> def wait_for_clean_9008(timeout=120):
>
>     """
>
>     Wait for device to enter clean 9008 mode via volume buttons.
>
>     Returns USB device object or None.
>
>     """
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print("CLEAN 9008 ENTRY INSTRUCTIONS:")
>
>     print("1. UNPLUG USB cable")
>
>     print("2. Press and hold BOTH VOLUME UP + VOLUME DOWN")
>
>     print("3. While holding, PLUG USB CABLE BACK IN")
>
>     print("4. Keep holding for 5-10 seconds")
>
>     print("=" * 60)
>
>     print(f"\nWaiting up to {timeout} seconds for 9008 device...")
>
>
>
>     start = time.time()
>
>     while time.time() - start < timeout:
>
>         dev = usb.core.find(idVendor=0x05C6, idProduct=0x9008)
>
>         if dev:
>
>             print(f"\n![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) 9008 FOUND! bus={dev.bus} addr={dev.address}")
>
>             return dev
>
>         if int(time.time() - start) % 10 == 0:
>
>             print(f"  {int(time.time() - start)}s...")
>
>         time.sleep(1)
>
>
>
>     print("\n![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No 9008 device found within timeout")
>
>     return None
>
>
>
> if __name__ == "__main__":
>
>     dev = wait_for_clean_9008()
>
>
> #### Script 2: Complete Flash (The One That Works)​
> python
>
> # root_redmagic.py
>
> import usb.core, usb.util
>
> import struct, time, os
>
>
>
> # ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
>
> LUN = 4
>
> VBMETA_SECTOR = 490260
>
> VBMETA_SECTORS = 16
>
> INITBOOT_SECTOR = 686048
>
> INITBOOT_SECTORS = 2048  # 8MB
>
>
>
> PROG_FILE = "devprg.melf"
>
> VBMETA_PATCHED = "vbmeta_b_patched.img"
>
> INITBOOT_PATCHED = "magisk_patched.img"
>
>
>
> # ========== USB SETUP ==========
>
> def setup_usb(dev):
>
>     """Configure USB endpoints for Sahara/firehose"""
>
>     try:
>
>         if dev.is_kernel_driver_active(0):
>
>             dev.detach_kernel_driver(0)
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     try:
>
>         dev.set_configuration()
>
>     except:
>
>         pass
>
>
>
>     cfg = dev.get_active_configuration()
>
>     intf = cfg[(0,0)]
>
>
>
>     ep_out = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_OUT
>
>     )
>
>     ep_in = usb.util.find_descriptor(
>
>         intf,
>
>         custom_match=lambda e: usb.util.endpoint_direction(e.bEndpointAddress) == usb.util.ENDPOINT_IN
>
>     )
>
>
>
>     return ep_out, ep_in
>
>
>
> def read_ep(ep, timeout=2000, size=4096):
>
>     """Safely read from endpoint"""
>
>     try:
>
>         return bytes(ep.read(size, timeout=timeout))
>
>     except:
>
>         return b''
>
>
>
> def write_ep(ep, data, timeout=5000):
>
>     """Safely write to endpoint"""
>
>     if isinstance(data, str):
>
>         data = data.encode()
>
>     try:
>
>         ep.write(data, timeout=timeout)
>
>         return True
>
>     except Exception as e:
>
>         print(f"  WRITE ERROR: {e}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
> # ========== SAHARA PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def sahara_upload(ep_out, ep_in, prog_data):
>
>     """
>
>     Upload programmer via Sahara.
>
>     Returns True if successful (38 chunks, DONE_RSP received)
>
>     """
>
>     print("\n=== SAHARA UPLOAD ===")
>
>
>
>     # Read HELLO
>
>     hello = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000, size=256)
>
>     if not hello or len(hello) < 24:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No Sahara HELLO received")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     cmd = struct.unpack('<I', hello[0:4])[0]
>
>     if cmd != 0x01:
>
>         print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Not HELLO: cmd=0x{cmd:x}")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     ver = struct.unpack('<I', hello[8:12])[0]
>
>     verc = struct.unpack('<I', hello[12:16])[0]
>
>     mode = struct.unpack('<I', hello[20:24])[0]
>
>     print(f"HELLO: v{ver}/{verc} mode={mode}")
>
>
>
>     # Send HELLO_RESP (ALL ZEROS - CRITICAL!)
>
>     resp = struct.pack('<IIIIIIIIIIII',
>
>                        0x02, 0x30, ver, verc,
>
>                        0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, resp):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Upload loop
>
>     chunks = 0
>
>     while True:
>
>         pkt = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>         if not pkt:
>
>             print("![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Timeout waiting for command")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         cmd = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[0:4])[0]
>
>
>
>         if cmd == 0x12:  # READ_DATA_64
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[16:24])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<Q', pkt[24:32])[0]
>
>             if chunks == 0:
>
>                 print(f"First READ_DATA_64: off={off} len={ln}")
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x03:  # READ_DATA
>
>             off = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             ln = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[16:20])[0]
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, prog_data[off![:eek:](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)ff+ln].ljust(ln, b'\xff'))
>
>             chunks += 1
>
>
>
>         elif cmd == 0x04:  # END_TRANSFER
>
>             status = struct.unpack('<I', pkt[12:16])[0]
>
>             print(f"END_TRANSFER: status={status} chunks={chunks}")
>
>
>
>             # Send DONE_REQ
>
>             write_ep(ep_out, struct.pack('<II', 0x05, 0x08))
>
>
>
>             # Read DONE_RSP
>
>             done = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000, size=256)
>
>             if done:
>
>                 done_cmd = struct.unpack('<I', done[0:4])[0]
>
>                 print(f"DONE_RSP: cmd=0x{done_cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>         else:
>
>             print(f"![⚠️](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/26a0.png) Unknown command: 0x{cmd:x}")
>
>             break
>
>
>
>     success = (chunks == 38)  # Known good count for devprg.melf
>
>     print(f"Sahara {'![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) SUCCESS' if success else '![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) FAILED'} ({chunks} chunks)")
>
>     return success
>
>
>
> # ========== FIREHOSE PROTOCOL ==========
>
> def firehose_configure(ep_out, ep_in):
>
>     """Send configure XML and wait for ACK"""
>
>     print("\n=== CONFIGURING FIREHOSE ===")
>
>
>
>     cfg_xml = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?><data><configure MemoryName="UFS" Verbose="0" AlwaysValidate="0" MaxDigestTableSizeInBytes="2048" MaxPayloadSizeToTargetInBytes="1048576" ZLPAwareHost="1" SkipStorageInit="0" SkipWrite="0" Oem="ZTE"/></data>'
>
>
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, cfg_xml):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Wait for ACK (up to 10s)
>
>     for i in range(20):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=1000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Configure ACK received")
>
>                 return True
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Configure NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.5)
>
>
>
>     print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No configure response")
>
>     return False
>
>
>
> def firehose_program(ep_out, ep_in, data, start_sector, num_sectors, name):
>
>     """
>
>     Flash data to partition.
>
>     CRITICAL: Send ALL data, then ONE ZLP at the end
>
>     """
>
>     print(f"\n=== PROGRAMMING {name} ===")
>
>     print(f"Start sector: {start_sector}, Sectors: {num_sectors}, Size: {len(data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     # Send program command
>
>     prog_xml = f'<?xml version="1.0" ?><data><program SECTOR_SIZE_IN_BYTES="4096" num_partition_sectors="{num_sectors}" physical_partition_number="{LUN}" start_sector="{start_sector}" filename="{name}"/></data>'
>
>
>
>     if not write_ep(ep_out, prog_xml):
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     # Wait for rawmode ACK
>
>     rawmode = False
>
>     for i in range(30):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=3000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:150]}")
>
>             if 'rawmode="true"' in txt.lower() and 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 rawmode = True
>
>                 break
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Program NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.2)
>
>
>
>     if not rawmode:
>
>         print("![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No rawmode ACK")
>
>         return False
>
>
>
>     print("![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) Rawmode ACK received, sending data...")
>
>
>
>     # Send ALL data continuously
>
>     sent = 0
>
>     chunk_size = 65536  # 64KB chunks for USB
>
>     while sent < len(data):
>
>         end = min(sent + chunk_size, len(data))
>
>         if not write_ep(ep_out, data[sent:end], timeout=30000):
>
>             print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) Write failed at {sent}/{len(data)}")
>
>             return False
>
>         sent = end
>
>         if sent % 262144 == 0 or sent == len(data):
>
>             print(f"  Sent {sent}/{len(data)} bytes")
>
>
>
>     # CRITICAL: Send Zero Length Packet at the very end
>
>     print("Sending ZLP...")
>
>     write_ep(ep_out, b"", timeout=1000)
>
>
>
>     # Wait for final ACK
>
>     print("Waiting for flash ACK...")
>
>     for i in range(60):
>
>         resp = read_ep(ep_in, timeout=5000)
>
>         if resp:
>
>             txt = resp.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
>
>             print(f"  {txt[:200]}")
>
>             if 'value="ACK"' in txt:
>
>                 print(f"![✅](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/2705.png) {name} flashed successfully!")
>
>                 return True
>
>             if 'value="NAK"' in txt:
>
>                 print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) {name} flash NAK")
>
>                 return False
>
>         time.sleep(0.5)
>
>
>
>     print(f"![❌](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/6.6/png/unicode/64/274c.png) No final ACK for {name}")
>
>     return False
>
>

> ### Troubleshooting​
>
> #### "No 9008 device found"​
> **Problem:** Volume button method didn't work
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Try these alternatives:
>
> 1. Let battery die completely, then try volume buttons
>
> 2. From fastboot: fastboot reboot edl
>
> 3. From ADB (if bootable): adb reboot edl
>
> 4. Use EDL test point (last resort - requires opening phone)
>
>
> #### Sahara upload fails (not 38 chunks)​
> **Problem:** Wrong programmer or corrupted file
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> powershell
>
> # Verify devprg.melf is correct
>
> python -c "
>
> data = open('devprg.melf','rb').read()
>
> print('Size:', len(data))
>
> print('ELF magic:', data[:4])
>
> print('Has firehose strings:', b'configure' in data)
>
> "
>
> # Should show: Size ~1.6MB, b'configure' found
>
>
> #### Configure NAK / No response​
> **Problem:** Programmer not starting firehose mode
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Ensure you entered **clean 9008** (volume buttons), NOT ZTE→9008
> - Try waiting 3 seconds after Sahara instead of 2
> - Check if USB reset happened (device should briefly disappear)
>
> #### Flash succeeds but phone won't boot​
> **Problem:** AVB still active or wrong partition
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
> python
>
> # Verify vbmeta patch
>
> with open('vbmeta_b_patched.img','rb') as f:
>
>     data = f.read()
>
> print(f"Flags at offset 12: {data[12:16].hex()}")
>
> # Should show: 02000000
>
>
> #### Phone stuck at "Your device is corrupt"​
> **Problem:** vbmeta verification still enabled
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Re-flash with proper vbmeta patch (flags=2)
> - Check if you flashed to correct slot (make sure it's _b)
> - Consider flashing both slots if unsure
>
> #### Windows can't find device after Sahara​
> **Problem:** USB re-enumeration timing
>
> **Solution:**
>
>
>
>
> - Use the script above - it reconnects properly
> - Don't use Zadig or change drivers - libusb backend works
> - If using Zadig, install WinUSB for 9008 mode
>
>
>
> ### FAQ​
>
> #### Q: Is devprg.melf the correct programmer?​
> **A:** Yes! It contains firehose protocol strings (configure, rawmode, program, UFS). The issue was never the programmer - it was USB re-enumeration.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Why doesn't ZTE → SWITCH_MODE work?​
> **A:** The ZTE crash handler leaves USB in a dirty state. After transition, the programmer's USB reset creates a new device that Windows takes 60+ seconds to enumerate - by then the programmer has crashed (8s watchdog).
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What's with the Zero Length Packet (ZLP)?​
> **A:** Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" expects a ZLP after data transfers that are exact multiples of USB packet size. 8MB (8388608 bytes) is a multiple of 512/1024, so a ZLP is required. Sending ZLP after every chunk corrupts the data.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Do I need to flash both slots?​
> **A:** For safety, flash only slot B if that's your active slot. Check with:
>
>
>
> bash
>
> # In fastboot
>
> fastboot getvar current-slot
>
> If unsure, you can flash both - just adjust sector addresses from GPT.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: What about other vbmeta partitions (system, vendor)?​
> **A:** The main vbmeta controls boot image verification. If you're only modifying init_boot, patching main vbmeta is sufficient. If you modify system/vendor later, you'll need to patch those too.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Will this work on other REDMAGIC models?​
> **A:** The principles apply, but partition addresses will differ. You'll need to dump GPT from your specific model first.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: My phone won't enter 9008 at all!​
> **A:** Last resort - EDL test point. Requires opening the phone and shorting specific pads. Check XDA for your model's test point location.
>
>
>
>
> #### Q: Is the bootloader unlocked after this?​
> **A:** No - this method bypasses the bootloader entirely via EDL. The bootloader remains locked. You're rooted with a locked bootloader, which is possible on Qualcomm devices via EDL.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> ### Partition Reference (REDMAGIC 10 Pro - NX789J)​
>
> #### LUN4 GPT (User Data/System Partitions)​
> text
>
> Partition           Start Sector    Sectors     Size
>
> ------------------  -------------   --------    --------
>
> xbl_b               184             15360       60MB
>
> abl_b               448832          256         1MB
>
> boot_b              683040          32768       128MB
>
> init_boot_b         686048          2048        8MB
>
> vbmeta_b            490260          16          64KB
>
> vbmeta_system_b     520120          16          64KB
>
> vbmeta_vendor_b     492584          16          64KB
>
>
> #### Critical Addresses for Rooting​
> python
>
> VBMETA_B = {
>
>     'lun': 4,
>
>     'start': 490260,
>
>     'sectors': 16,
>
>     'size': 65536
>
> }
>
>
>
> INIT_BOOT_B = {
>
>     'lun': 4,
>
>     'start': 686048,
>
>     'sectors': 2048,
>
>     'size': 8388608
>
> }
>
>
>
> **The most important lesson:** Don't trust the 8-second window. The programmer is alive for ~8 seconds, but you have to catch it in the first 2 seconds after USB re-enumeration. The volume button method gives you a clean state where the programmer stays alive and the USB handle remains valid.
>
>
>
> **The ZLP (Zero Length Packet) issue** cost us 10+ hours. Firehose with ZLPAwareHost="1" is strict about protocol - one ZLP at the end, not after every chunk.
>
>
>
> **vbmeta is NOT optional** - if you flash a modified init_boot without patching vbmeta, you'll get "device is corrupt" every time. Patch flags to 0x02.
>
>
>
> **The programmer IS correct** - devprg.melf from ZTE dump mode is a valid firehose programmer. Don't waste time searching for another one.
>
>
>
>
>
> *This guide represents 26+ hours of debugging across 50+ scripts, 3 USB protocol analyzers, and 2 near-brick scares. I will share freely on XDA and help others avoid the same pitfalls.*
>
>

> **Last Updated:** February 2025
>
> **Device:** REDMAGIC 10 Pro (NX789J)
>
> **Android Version:** 15
>
> **Kernel:** GKI compatible

Any modified or patched vbmeta **fails signature verification, 100% lead a brick without resigning, **

There are only a few scenarios where it *might* work like Engineering firmware / factory devices.
